```java
    void begForImperialScript(RoomProfile rp, ZoneType zt) {
        if (zt == ZoneType.MUTANT_WARRENS || zt == ZoneType.MUTANT_SEWER_CAMP || zt == ZoneType.CULTIST_SEWER_CAMP) {
            lastScavengeReport = "That's a bad idea. What, do you want to get shanked? Begging is disabled in mutant and cultist zones.";
            logEvent(lastScavengeReport);
            showTimedAlert("SCAVENGE RESULT", lastScavengeReport, 3600);
            DebugLog.audit("BEG_DISABLED", "zone="+zt.label+" room="+rp.name+" state="+stateSummary());
            return;
        }
        int payoutBase = beggingPayoutBase(zt);
        int risk = beggingArbitesRisk(zt);
        int chance = Math.max(8, Math.min(85, payoutBase + stat("Charm",5)*3 + (rp.name.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("queue")?8:0)));
        int roll = rng.nextInt(100)+1;
        int riskRoll = rng.nextInt(100)+1;
        DebugLog.audit("BEG_SCRIPT", "zone="+zt.label+" room="+rp.name+" roll="+roll+" chance="+chance+" riskRoll="+riskRoll+" risk="+risk+" state="+stateSummary());
        if (riskRoll <= risk) {
            int fine = Math.min(countMoney(), Math.max(1, risk/12));
            if (fine > 0) spendImperialScript(fine);
            suspicion += Math.max(1, risk/20);
            lastScavengeReport = "Civic Wardens attention catches your begging. Fine: " + fine + " script. Suspicion rises to " + suspicion + ".";
            logEvent(lastScavengeReport);
        } else if (roll <= chance) {
            int amount = Math.max(1, 1 + rng.nextInt(Math.max(2, payoutBase/12 + 1)));
            addImperialScript(amount);
            purgePhysicalScriptInstances("begging payout must remain tracked cash");
            lastScavengeReport = "Begged for Concord Script in " + zt.label + ": gained " + amount + " tracked cash, not an inventory item.";
            logEvent(lastScavengeReport);
        } else {
            lastScavengeReport = "Begged for Concord Script in " + zt.label + ": nothing but contempt.";
            logEvent(lastScavengeReport);
        }
        showTimedAlert("SCAVENGE RESULT", lastScavengeReport, 3600);
        for (int i=0;i<Math.max(2, 6 - stat("Agility",5)/3);i++) advanceTurn("begs for Concord Script.");
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void restOneHourOnUnclaimedFurniture(int tx, int ty, char tile) {
        int rid = world.roomIdAt(tx, ty);
        if (rid < 0 || isInClaimedRoom(tx, ty)) { logEvent("This rest spot is not an unclaimed public room feature."); return; }
        int chanceKick = 25 + Math.max(0, gangHeat/3) + (world.roomFaction(rid)==Faction.NONE ? 0 : 15);
        int roll = rng.nextInt(100);
        DebugLog.audit("PUBLIC_REST", "tile="+tile+" room="+rid+" kickChance="+chanceKick+" roll="+roll+" state="+stateSummary());
        showTimedAlert("YOU FELL ASLEEP IN PUBLIC!", "You curl up on unclaimed furniture for a desperate hour. Anyone passing by may decide this is their problem, your problem, or an opportunity.", 4200);
        for (int i=0;i<6;i++) advanceTurn("rests uneasily on unclaimed furniture.");
        if (roll < chanceKick) {
            fatigue = Math.min(25, fatigue + 1);
            logEvent("You try to rest for an hour, but someone kicks you out before it does much good. Fatigue +1 from interrupted sleep.");
        } else {
            int old = fatigue; fatigue = Math.max(0, fatigue - 1);
            logEvent("You steal one hour of rough rest on public furniture. Fatigue " + old + "->" + fatigue + ".");
        }
    }
```

```java
    void prayImperialForgivenessService() {
        if (activeConversationNpc == null || !activeConversationNpc.isProtectedCleric()) { logEvent("Prayer blocked: no head cleric is hearing confession."); return; }
        final int hours = 24;
        final int turnsSpent = hours * TURNS_PER_HOUR;
        int oldFood = food, oldWater = water, oldSleep = sleepNeed, oldFatigue = fatigue, oldSuspicion = suspicion, oldHeat = gangHeat;
        food = Math.max(0, food - 3);
        water = Math.max(0, water - 3);
        fatigue = Math.min(25, fatigue + 6);
        sleepNeed = Math.min(MAX_SLEEP_NEED, sleepNeed + turnsSpent);
        advancePlayerAndWorldTime(turnsSpent, "Concord forgiveness prayer service");
        suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion - 8);
        gangHeat = Math.max(0, gangHeat - 3);
        int restored = 0;
        Faction[] civil = {Faction.CIVIC_LEDGER_OFFICE, Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS, Faction.IMPERIAL_GUARD, Faction.MINISTORUM, Faction.SORORITAS, Faction.MECHANIST_COLLEGIA, Faction.MECHANICUS_CLOISTER_RED, Faction.MECHANICUS_CLOISTER_RUST, Faction.MECHANICUS_CLOISTER_VOID, Faction.HIVER, Faction.HIVER_BLOCK_AUREL, Faction.HIVER_BLOCK_MARROW, Faction.HIVER_BLOCK_SUMPLEDGER, Faction.NOBLE, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_VARN, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_KASTOR, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_MORVAIN, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_CYRA, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_DRAKE, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_TOLL, Faction.NOBLE_HOUSE_OSSUARY};
        for (Faction f : civil) {
            int old = factionStanding.getOrDefault(f, 0);
            int neu = old < 0 ? Math.min(0, old + 12) : Math.min(35, old + 3);
            factionStanding.put(f, neu);
            restored += Math.max(0, neu - old);
            temporaryHostileTurns.put(f, Math.max(0, temporaryHostileTurns.getOrDefault(f,0) - turnsSpent));
        }
        if (food <= 0 || water <= 0) { wounds++; pain = Math.min(10, pain + 1); }
        conversationBranch = activeConversationNpc.name + ": Twenty-four hours. Knees, hunger, thirst, and sleep offered up. Forgiveness is not innocence, but it is a receipt.";
        lastConversation = conversationBranch;
        logConversation("MINISTORUM_FORGIVENESS", conversationBranch);
        logEvent("CONCORD FORGIVENESS RITE: 24h prayer completed. Food " + oldFood + "->" + food + ", water " + oldWater + "->" + water + ", sleep " + oldSleep + "->" + sleepNeed + ", fatigue " + oldFatigue + "->" + fatigue + ", suspicion " + oldSuspicion + "->" + suspicion + ", heat " + oldHeat + "->" + gangHeat + ", civil standing restored +" + restored + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("MINISTORUM_FORGIVENESS", "cleric=" + activeConversationNpc.name + " hours=" + hours + " restored=" + restored + " food=" + oldFood + "->" + food + " water=" + oldWater + "->" + water + " sleep=" + oldSleep + "->" + sleepNeed + " fatigue=" + oldFatigue + "->" + fatigue + " suspicion=" + oldSuspicion + "->" + suspicion + " heat=" + oldHeat + "->" + gangHeat + " state=" + stateSummary());
        updateSensoryModel("after Ministorum forgiveness prayer");
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void tradeBuySelected() {
        if (activeTrader == null) { tradeBuySupply(); return; }
        TradeOffer offer = selectedTradeOffer();
        if (offer == null) { lastTradeReport = "No selected trade offer."; logEvent(lastTradeReport); return; }
        int price = activeTrader.buyPrice(offer);
        if (inventoryWeight() + 1 > carryCapacity()) {
            lastTradeReport = "Purchase blocked: carried inventory would exceed Strength-derived carry capacity. " + tradeBuyTransferPreviewLine(offer, price);
            logEvent(lastTradeReport);
            return;
        }
        if (!spendImperialScript(price)) {
            lastTradeReport = activeTrader.name + " taps the price slate. Need " + price + " concord script.";
            logEvent(lastTradeReport); DebugLog.audit("TRADE_BUY_FAIL", lastTradeReport + " state=" + stateSummary()); return;
        }
        ItemActionResult bought = buyTraderOfferIntoInventory(activeTrader, offer);
        if (!bought.success) {
            addImperialScript(price);
            lastTradeReport = "Purchase failed after payment authorization; funds returned. " + bought.playerText;
            logEvent(lastTradeReport);
            DebugLog.warn("TRADE_BUY_FAIL", bought.auditText + " state=" + stateSummary());
            return;
        }
        lastTradeReport = "ITEM PURCHASED: Bought " + offer.name + " for " + price + " concord script from " + activeTrader.name + ". " + (bought.provenance == null ? "Origin transferred without detailed ledger." : bought.provenance.summary());
        logEvent(lastTradeReport); logConversation("TRADE_BUY", lastTradeReport); gainXp("Commerce", 1, "purchase");
        DebugLog.audit("TRADE_OPTION", "BUY item=" + offer.name + " price=" + price + " trader=" + activeTrader.name + " instance=" + bought.itemInstanceId + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("buys " + offer.name + ".");
    }
```

```java
    void tradeSellSelected() {
        if (activeTrader == null) { tradeSellScrap(); return; }
        String item = selectedInventoryItemName();
        if (item == null || item.equals("Concord Script")) { lastTradeReport = "Select a carried item that is not money before selling."; logEvent(lastTradeReport); return; }
```

```java
    void tradeHaggle() {
        if (activeTrader == null) { lastTradeReport = "No trader is currently engaged for haggling."; logEvent(lastTradeReport); return; }
        activeTrader.haggleAttempts++;
        int charm = stat("Charm", 5);
        int chance = Math.max(5, Math.min(92, 30 + charm * 5 - activeTrader.haggleAttempts * 10));
        int roll = rng.nextInt(100) + 1;
        if (roll <= chance) {
            int gain = 5 + rng.nextInt(11);
            activeTrader.discountPct = Math.min(45, activeTrader.discountPct + gain);
            conversationBranch = activeTrader.name + ": Fine. I shave " + gain + "% from the slate. Do not smile like you earned it.";
            lastTradeReport = "Haggle succeeded: roll " + roll + " <= " + chance + ". Discount now " + activeTrader.discountPct + "%.";
        } else if (roll > chance + 30 || activeTrader.haggleAttempts >= 3) {
            int penalty = 5 + rng.nextInt(11);
            activeTrader.discountPct = 0;
            activeTrader.markupPct = Math.min(50, activeTrader.markupPct + penalty);
            conversationBranch = activeTrader.name + ": That tone just cost you. Prices rise " + penalty + "%.";
            lastTradeReport = "Haggle angered trader: roll " + roll + " > " + chance + ". Discounts cleared; markup now " + activeTrader.markupPct + "%.";
        } else {
            conversationBranch = activeTrader.name + ": No. Ask again and I may remember my larger prices.";
            lastTradeReport = "Haggle failed safely: roll " + roll + " > " + chance + ". Further attempts are risky.";
        }
        logEvent(lastTradeReport); logConversation("TRADE_HAGGLE", conversationBranch);
        DebugLog.audit("TRADE_OPTION", "HAGGLE roll=" + roll + " chance=" + chance + " attempts=" + activeTrader.haggleAttempts + " discount=" + activeTrader.discountPct + " markup=" + activeTrader.markupPct + " trader=" + activeTrader.name + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("haggles with " + activeTrader.name + ".");
    }
```

```java
    void purgePhysicalScriptInstances(String reason) {
        ArrayList<String> removeIds = new ArrayList<>();
        for (ItemInstance inst : itemInstances.values()) {
            if (inst != null && "Concord Script".equalsIgnoreCase(inst.displayName)) removeIds.add(inst.id);
        }
        if (!removeIds.isEmpty()) {
            for (String id : removeIds) itemInstances.remove(id);
            for (ContainerRecord c : itemContainers.values()) if (c != null) c.itemInstanceIds.removeAll(removeIds);
            DebugLog.audit("SCRIPT_INSTANCE_PURGE", "removed=" + removeIds.size() + " reason=" + reason + " state=" + stateSummary());
        }
    }
```

```java
    void applyAuthorityFacilityInspectionFromNews() {
        if (world == null || !baseClaimed || turn < authorityFacilityInspectionCooldownUntilTurn) return;
        if (turn % (3 * TURNS_PER_HOUR) != 0) return;
        boolean civilOrNoble = world.zoneType == ZoneType.NEUTRAL_CIVILIAN_FLOOR || world.zoneType == ZoneType.HAB_STACK || world.zoneType == ZoneType.NOBLE_SERVICE_SPINE || world.zoneType == ZoneType.SECTOR_GOVERNORS_MANSION || world.zoneType == ZoneType.ADMINISTRATUM_ARCHIVE || world.zoneType == ZoneType.IMPERIAL_NEWS_NETWORK || world.floor >= 5;
        if (!civilOrNoble) return;
        int day = currentInnDay();
        int publicHeat = 0;
        for (PlayerNewsEvent ev : playerNewsEvents) if (ev != null && ev.shouldBePublicBy(day) && ev.ageDays(day) <= 2) publicHeat += Math.max(1, ev.severity);
        int openIllegal = illegalBusinessCount();
        int unlicensedFacilities = 0;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if (obj != null && obj.isBusinessAsset() && obj.businessOpen && !obj.permittedBusiness) unlicensedFacilities++;
        int pressure = suspicion + gangHeat/2 + publicHeat + openIllegal * 5 + unlicensedFacilities * 4;
        if (pressure < 18) return;
        int chance = Math.max(8, Math.min(70, pressure - baseSecurityRating() * 2));
        if (rng.nextInt(100) >= chance) {
            authorityFacilityInspectionCooldownUntilTurn = turn + 4 * TURNS_PER_HOUR;
            lastAuthorityFacilityInspectionReport = "Authority review noted public reporting but delayed inspection. Pressure " + pressure + ", chance " + chance + "%.";
            DebugLog.audit("AUTHORITY_FACILITY_INSPECTION_DELAY", lastAuthorityFacilityInspectionReport + " state=" + stateSummary());
            return;
        }
        int fine = Math.max(10, 20 + openIllegal * 35 + unlicensedFacilities * 25 + publicHeat * 3 + rng.nextInt(60));
        int paid = Math.min(carriedScript, fine);
        carriedScript -= paid;
        int unpaid = fine - paid;
        suspicion += 2 + openIllegal;
        gangHeat += Math.max(0, openIllegal - 1);
        authorityFacilityInspectionCooldownUntilTurn = turn + (18 + rng.nextInt(18)) * TURNS_PER_HOUR;
        lastAuthorityFacilityInspectionReport = "Authority facility inspection follows recent INN attention. Fine " + fine + " script, paid " + paid + (unpaid > 0 ? ", unpaid docket " + unpaid : "") + ". Illegal/open facilities " + openIllegal + ", public heat " + publicHeat + ".";
        logEvent("AUTHORITY INSPECTION: " + lastAuthorityFacilityInspectionReport);
        DebugLog.audit("AUTHORITY_FACILITY_INSPECTION", lastAuthorityFacilityInspectionReport + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void recoverOldNewspaperAt(int tx, int ty) {
        MapObjectState m = mapObjectAt(tx, ty, AssetIntegrationDisciplineAuthority.DISCARDED_NEWSPRINT_SOURCE);
        if (m == null) return;
        int age = Math.max(1, currentInnDay() - safeParseInt(MapObjectState.itemNameFromStock(m.stockState), currentInnDay()-1));
        String item = age <= 1 ? "Yesterday's INN newspaper" : (age <= 6 ? "Old INN newspaper" : "Useless paper mush");

        addInventoryItem(item, ItemProvenanceRecord.of(item, Faction.INN, "discarded public newsprint source", world, turn, "old newspaper day " + MapObjectState.itemNameFromStock(m.stockState), "recovered from trash or floor litter"));
        world.mapObjects.remove(m);
        if (world.inBounds(tx, ty)) { char old = MapObjectState.underlyingTileFromStock(m.stockState); if (old == 0 || old == 'o' || old == '1') old = '.'; world.tiles[tx][ty] = old; }
        logEvent("Recovered " + item + ". Yesterday's public truth is now trash, which is still more useful than most official signage.");

        repaint();
```

```java
    void readInventoryNewspaper(String item) {
        int day = currentInnDay();
        String low = item == null ? "" : item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        int issueDay = day;
        if (low.contains("yesterday")) issueDay = Math.max(0, day - 1);
        else if (low.contains("old")) issueDay = Math.max(0, day - 2 - Math.abs(Objects.hash(item, seed)) % 5);
        else if (low.contains("mush")) { logEvent("The paper mush has surrendered all information to damp, boot grease, and time."); advanceTurn("tries to read paper mush."); return; }
        String issue = ImperialNewsNetworkApi.ensureDailyIssue(this, issueDay, rng);
        logEvent("NEWSPAPER day " + issueDay + ": " + issue);
        lastInnNewsIssue = issue;
        gainXp("Investigation", 1, "read public faction news");
        DebugLog.audit("INN_READ_PAPER", "item=" + item + " issueDay=" + issueDay + " issue=" + issue + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("reads a newspaper.");
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void interactLightSwitchAt(int tx, int ty) {
        MapObjectState m = mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "light-switch");
        if (world == null || m == null) return;
        String group = ZoneLightSourceRecord.groupFromStock(m.stockState);
        if (group == null || group.isBlank()) { logEvent("The light switch has no readable circuit tag. The fixture obeys no obvious authority."); return; }
        boolean anyOn = false;
        int changed = 0;
        for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : world.lightSources) if (l != null && group.equals(l.groupId) && l.on) anyOn = true;
        boolean newState = !anyOn;
        for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : world.lightSources) if (l != null && group.equals(l.groupId)) { l.on = newState; changed++; }
        if (changed > 0) {
            m.stockState = MapObjectState.setStockFlag(m.stockState, "on", String.valueOf(newState));
            lightingCacheTurn = -999999;
            sensoryCacheWorld = null;
            lastZoneLightingReport = "LIGHT SWITCH: " + changed + " fixture(s) on circuit " + group + " turned " + (newState ? "on" : "off") + ".";
            logEvent(lastZoneLightingReport);
            DebugLog.audit("LIGHT_SWITCH", "group=" + group + " on=" + newState + " changed=" + changed + " at=" + tx + "," + ty + " state=" + stateSummary());
            advanceTurn("toggles a local light switch.");
        } else {
            logEvent("The switch clicks, but no surviving light answers the insult.");
        }
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void interactAt(int tx, int ty) {
        if (world == null) { DebugLog.warn("INTERACT", "interactAt called without world. " + stateSummary()); logEvent("Cannot interact: no active world."); return; }
        if (tx < 0 || ty < 0 || tx >= world.w || ty >= world.h) { DebugLog.warn("INTERACT", "target out of bounds. " + stateSummary()); logEvent("Cannot interact: target out of bounds."); return; }
        if (Math.abs(tx-playerX) > 1 || Math.abs(ty-playerY) > 1) { logEvent("Cannot interact: target must be adjacent to your character."); return; }
        NpcEntity npc = world.npcAt(tx, ty);
        if (npc != null) {
            if (npc.isPetActor()) { petNpcAt(tx, ty, false); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
            if (npc.isAnimalActor()) { logEvent("PET: " + animalContactBlockedLine(npc)); advanceTurn("checks an animal's mood."); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
            talkToNpc(npc); advanceTurn("speaks with " + npc.name + "."); return;
        }
        BaseObject obj = baseObjectAt(tx, ty);
        if (obj != null) { interactBaseObject(obj); advanceTurn("interacts with " + obj.name + "."); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "planted-explosive") != null) { disarmExplosiveAt(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "bank-vault") != null) { openBankVaultAt(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "bank-alarm-panel") != null) { tamperBankAlarmPanelAt(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "bank-terminal") != null) { logEvent("BANK: " + bankTerminalPreview(tx, ty)); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, AssetIntegrationDisciplineAuthority.INN_NEWSPAPER_DISPENSER) != null) { interactNewsVendingMachine(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, AssetIntegrationDisciplineAuthority.DISCARDED_NEWSPRINT_SOURCE) != null) { recoverOldNewspaperAt(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "broadcast-device") != null) { interactBroadcastDevice(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (mapObjectAt(tx, ty, "light-switch") != null) { interactLightSwitchAt(tx, ty); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (RoomFixtureInteractionAuthority.tryInteract(this, tx, ty)) { updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (FrontageFixtureInteractionAuthority.tryInteract(this, tx, ty)) { updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (RoadTransitFixtureInteractionAuthority.tryInteract(this, tx, ty)) { updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        char here = world.tiles[tx][ty];
        DebugLog.audit("INTERACT", "tile=" + here + " at " + tx + "," + ty + " desc=" + describeTile(here));
        if (isFactionJournalObjectAt(tx, ty)) { readFactionJournalAt(tx, ty); advanceTurn("reads a faction journal ledger."); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        if (isDoorTile(here)) { interactDoorAt(tx, ty, here); updatePendingInteractionSummary(); return; }
        switch (here) {
            case 'g':
                gangHeat += 2;
                logEvent("You parley with gangers. They smell weakness, profit, and possibly soup.");
                break;
            case 'm':
                logEvent("The mutant watches you. Not hostile yet. Not safe either.");
                break;
            case 'R':
                logEvent("The rogue machine twitches. Reserved interaction: repair, hack, flee, or dismantle.");
                break;
            case 'A':
                suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion - 1);
                logEvent("You present yourself to Civic Wardens authority. Paperwork becomes a weapon pointed both ways.");
                break;
            case '1': case '2': case '3': case '4': case '5':
                interactVendingMachine(tx, ty, here);
                return;
            case 'Y': case 'J': case 'B': case 'K': case 'O': case 'Z': case 'P': case 'F': case 'U':
                interactEmergencyMachine(tx, ty, here);
                return;
            case 'I': case 'H':
                interactShrine(tx, ty, here);
                return;
            case 'T':
                openDepotTrader(tx, ty);
                break;
            case 'Q':
                logEvent(governorPreview(tx, ty));
                logEvent("Choose BRIBE GOVERNOR or ATTACK GOVERNOR from the interaction command list.");
                break;
            case 'D': case 'S': case 'v': case 'E':
                interactIntermapTransit(tx, ty, here);
                return;
            case 'C':
                logEvent("Clinic found. Present services: inspection, triage signposting, antiseptic smells, and malpractice with incense.");
                break;
            case 'q':
                talkToFactionRepresentative();
                break;
            case 'o':
                if (isFactionJournalObjectAt(tx, ty)) { readFactionJournalAt(tx, ty); return; }
                interactContractObject(tx, ty);
                return;
            case 'r':
                interactCorpseContainer(tx, ty);
                return;
            case 'b': case 'h': case 'n':
                restOneHourOnUnclaimedFurniture(tx, ty, here);
                return;
            default:
                if (isInClaimedRoom(tx, ty)) {
                    logEvent("You inspect your claimed room. Built objects=" + baseObjects.size() + ", stored items=" + baseStorage.size() + ".");
                } else {
                    logEvent("You search the adjacent room tile. Dust, rivets, old blood, and maybe one useful screw.");
                    if (inventoryWeight() + 1 <= carryCapacity()) addInventoryItem("Scrap bit", ItemProvenanceRecord.found("Scrap bit", world, turn, "adjacent room search"));
                    else logEvent("You find scrap but cannot carry more bulk.");
                }
        }
        advanceTurn("interacts with the surroundings.");
        updatePendingInteractionSummary();
    }
```

```java
    void interactDoorAt(int tx, int ty, char door) {
        int intellect = stat("Intellect", 5), mechanics = stat("Mechanics", 5), strength = stat("Strength", 5);
        String label = door=='/'?"open archway":(door=='|'?"hinged scrap door":(door=='L'?"locked or chained door":(door=='V'?"ventilation panel":(door=='X'?"electronic security door":"sealed vault door"))));
        if (door == '/') { logEvent("The open archway offers no barrier. You pass through if you dare."); return; }

        boolean mechanicalTools = countInventory("Lockpicks")>0 || countInventory("Tool bundle")>0 || countInventory("Mechanist Collegia tool roll")>0;
        boolean electronicTools = countInventory("Hacking tools")>0 || countInventory("Mechanist Collegia tool roll")>0 || countDataSpikes()>0 || countInventory("Keycard")>0;
        boolean secureVaultKey = countInventory("Secure vault key")>0 || countInventory("Vault key")>0;

        if (door == 'Z') {
            if (!secureVaultKey) {
                logEvent("The sealed vault door refuses ordinary tampering. It requires a Secure vault key likely held by a high-ranking individual in this zone.");
                DebugLog.audit("VAULT_KEY_REQUIRED", "door="+label+" at="+tx+","+ty+" keys="+countInventory("Secure vault key")+" state="+stateSummary());
                advanceTurn("studies a sealed vault door.");
                return;
            }
            world.tiles[tx][ty] = '/';
            logEvent("Secure vault key accepted. The sealed vault door opens with the weary contempt of expensive machinery.");
            DebugLog.audit("VAULT_UNLOCK", "door="+label+" at="+tx+","+ty+" usedSecureVaultKey=true state="+stateSummary());
            advanceTurn("unlocks a vault door.");
            return;
        }

        if (door == 'X') {
            if (countInventory("Keycard") > 0) {
                world.tiles[tx][ty] = '/';
                logEvent("Keycard accepted. The electronic security door opens.");
                DebugLog.audit("ELECTRONIC_DOOR_KEYCARD", "door="+label+" at="+tx+","+ty+" state="+stateSummary());
                advanceTurn("uses a keycard.");
                return;
            }
            if (countDataSpikes() <= 0 && countInventory("Hacking tools") <= 0) {
                logEvent("Electronic security door. Requires a Keycard, Hacking tools, or a Data spike. Data spikes are consumed on hack attempts.");
                DebugLog.audit("ELECTRONIC_DOOR_NEEDS_ACCESS", "door="+label+" at="+tx+","+ty+" dataSpikes="+countDataSpikes()+" state="+stateSummary());
                advanceTurn("checks an electronic lock.");
                return;
            }
            boolean usedSpike = false;
            if (countDataSpikes() > 0) { consumeDataSpike(); usedSpike = true; }
            int difficulty = 18;
            int roll = intellect + mechanics/2 + rng.nextInt(20) + 1 + (countInventory("Hacking tools")>0 ? 4 : 0) + (usedSpike ? 6 : 0);
            if (roll >= difficulty) {
                world.tiles[tx][ty] = '/';
                logEvent((usedSpike?"Data spike burned. ":"") + "Electronic lock bypassed with Intellect-assisted hacking. Roll " + roll + " >= " + difficulty + ".");
                DebugLog.audit("ELECTRONIC_DOOR_HACK", "door="+label+" at="+tx+","+ty+" roll="+roll+" diff="+difficulty+" dataSpikeConsumed="+usedSpike+" state="+stateSummary());
            } else {
                suspicion += 1;
                logEvent((usedSpike?"Data spike burned. ":"") + "Electronic bypass failed. Roll " + roll + " < " + difficulty + ". Suspicion +1.");
                DebugLog.audit("ELECTRONIC_DOOR_HACK_FAIL", "door="+label+" at="+tx+","+ty+" roll="+roll+" diff="+difficulty+" dataSpikeConsumed="+usedSpike+" state="+stateSummary());
            }
            advanceTurn("attempts electronic door access.");
            return;
        }

        int difficulty = (door=='|'?8:(door=='L'?14:(door=='V'?16:22)));
        int score = intellect + mechanics + strength/2;
        int roll = rng.nextInt(12) + 1 + score + (mechanicalTools ? 5 : 0) + (electronicTools && door=='V' ? 3 : 0);
        DebugLog.audit("DOOR_INTERACT", "door=" + label + " at=" + tx + "," + ty + " roll=" + roll + " difficulty=" + difficulty + " mechanicalTools=" + mechanicalTools + " electronicTools=" + electronicTools + " state=" + stateSummary());
        if (roll >= difficulty) {
            world.tiles[tx][ty] = '/';
            logEvent("Door opened: " + label + ". It no longer blocks line of sight.");
        } else {
            logEvent("Door access failed: " + label + ". Need tools, key, lockpicks, hacking tools, Data spike for electronic locks, or better checks. Roll " + roll + " < " + difficulty + ".");
            if (door == 'V') fatigue = Math.min(25, fatigue + 1);
        }
        advanceTurn("works the door access mechanism.");
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1115-1129
Kind: method
Name: interactZoneEdgeDoor
SHA256: e30ac5fd7945ef8d89a931d70d2cb7c6ebdfb4472694dc96e8f280a7b0de962a

```java
    void interactZoneEdgeDoor(int tx, int ty) {
        if (atlas == null || world == null) { logEvent("No sector atlas available for zone transition."); return; }
        String dir = edgeDirection(tx, ty);
        int oldZx = atlas.zoneX, oldZy = atlas.zoneY;
        int nzx = oldZx, nzy = oldZy;
        if ("N".equals(dir)) nzy--; else if ("S".equals(dir)) nzy++; else if ("W".equals(dir)) nzx--; else if ("E".equals(dir)) nzx++;
        if (nzx < 1 || nzx > 3 || nzy < 1 || nzy > 3) {
            logEvent("The double doors grind open on the void between walls: bottomless gangways, dead maintenance crawls, and spaces not meant for human lungs. You do not go there.");
            DebugLog.audit("ZONE_TRANSITION_BLOCKED", "dir="+dir+" fromZone="+oldZx+","+oldZy+" sector="+atlas.sectorX+","+atlas.sectorY+" state="+stateSummary());
            advanceTurn("checks a dead-end maintenance-bulkhead double door.");
            return;
        }
        atlas.zoneX = nzx; atlas.zoneY = nzy;
        loadAtlasWorld("zone edge door " + dir + " from " + oldZx + "," + oldZy + " to " + nzx + "," + nzy, oppositeEdgeSpawn(dir, tx, ty));
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1220-1262
Kind: method
Name: maybeRollZoneTransitionEvent
SHA256: 68ba5c7059051ea0c5daf4b8cfb277d4532ad4a634650a9e67d37d4fddc34ca2

```java
    String maybeRollZoneTransitionEvent(String reason) {
        if (world == null || active == null) return "";
        int visits = active.zoneVisitCounts.getOrDefault(world.zoneType.label, 0) + 1;
        active.zoneVisitCounts.put(world.zoneType.label, visits);
        int baseChance = 18 + Math.min(20, visits * 2);
        if (atlas != null && atlas.floor <= 2) baseChance += 8;
        if (equippedClothing != null && equippedClothing.alignedFaction == Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS && (world.zoneType == ZoneType.GANGER_TURF || world.zoneType == ZoneType.MUTANT_WARRENS)) baseChance += 10;
        int roll = rng.nextInt(100);
        if (roll >= baseChance) { lastTransitionEvent = "No event. roll=" + roll + " chance=" + baseChance; return ""; }
        String[] benign = {
            "A maintenance procession passes in the distance, lamps bobbing like tired insects.",
            "A child watches you from a vent grille, then vanishes before the question can form.",
            "A vox-speaker coughs three words of a sermon before dying into static.",
            "A freight chain rattles somewhere behind the wall, dragging unseen tonnage through the arcology bones.",
            "Someone has chalked a warning on the doorframe. The spelling is poor. The fear is not."
        };
        int rarity = rng.nextInt(100);
        String result;
        if (rarity < 70) {
            result = "Zone event: " + benign[rng.nextInt(benign.length)];
        } else if (rarity < 86) {
            String item = (world.zoneType == ZoneType.SEWER_CONDUIT || world.zoneType == ZoneType.MUTANT_SEWER_CAMP) ? "Sealed water ration" : "Emergency ration";
            addInventoryItem(item, ItemProvenanceRecord.found(item, world, turn, "threshold cache"));
            result = "Uncommon zone event: you find " + item + " wedged near the threshold.";
        } else if (rarity < 95) {
            Faction f = world.npcFactionForRoom(0);
            factionStanding.put(f, factionStanding.getOrDefault(f,0)+1);
            result = "Rare zone event: a fleeting contact gives you a nod. " + f.label + " standing +1.";
        } else {
            Point adj = adjacentOpenNearPlayer();
            if (adj != null) {
                NpcEntity hostile = NpcEntity.create(world.npcFactionForRoom(0), world.zoneType, adj.x, adj.y, rng);
                hostile.state = "HOSTILE";
                world.npcs.add(hostile);
                result = "Hostile zone event: something was waiting by the threshold. " + hostile.name + " appears nearby.";
            } else {
                result = "Rare zone event: hostile movement echoes nearby, but no creature finds a clean approach.";
            }
        }
        lastTransitionEvent = result + " roll=" + roll + " chance=" + baseChance + " rarity=" + rarity;
        DebugLog.audit("ZONE_TRANSITION_EVENT", lastTransitionEvent);
        return result;
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1271-1286
Kind: method
Name: spawnPointForTransition
SHA256: c92e60e7afafcfe76c75334c2411f146992b8cc5f58bb93a09ec46f2944d148b

```java
    Point spawnPointForTransition(Point edgeHint) {
        if (world == null) return new Point(2,2);
        if (edgeHint == null) return world.startPoint();
        if (pendingTransitionReturnEdge != null && !pendingTransitionReturnEdge.isEmpty()) {
            char edge = pendingTransitionReturnEdge.charAt(0);
            Point p = world.returnEdgeSpawn(edge, edgeHint);
            DebugLog.audit("EDGE_RETURN_SPAWN", "returnEdge=" + edge + " sourceHint=" + edgeHint.x + "," + edgeHint.y + " spawn=" + p.x + "," + p.y + " zone=" + world.zoneCoordText() + " layer=" + world.layerText());
            return p;
        }
        // Legacy sentinel hints from older saves/builds: still resolve to an edge-biased spawn.
        if (edgeHint.x == -1 && edgeHint.y == -2) return world.edgeSpawn('S');
        if (edgeHint.x == -1 && edgeHint.y == -3) return world.edgeSpawn('N');
        if (edgeHint.x == -2 && edgeHint.y == -1) return world.edgeSpawn('E');
        if (edgeHint.x == -3 && edgeHint.y == -1) return world.edgeSpawn('W');
        return world.nearestWalkableTo(edgeHint.x, edgeHint.y);
    }
```

```java
    void claimBaseHere() {
        if (world == null) return;
        int rid = world.roomIdAt(playerX, playerY);
        if (rid < 0) { logEvent("You can only claim an actual room, not a corridor or wall seam."); return; }
        baseClaimed = true;
        baseX = playerX; baseY = playerY; claimedRoomId = rid;
        suspicion += 2; gangHeat += 1;
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_CLAIM", "claimedRoom=" + claimedRoomId + " at=" + baseX + "," + baseY + " state=" + stateSummary());
        logEvent("Room claimed at " + baseX + "," + baseY + " as friendly territory. The law will want paperwork. The gangs will want contents.");
        recordPlayerNewsEvent("room-claim", "claimed room " + claimedRoomId, Faction.NONE, "new private foothold reported in " + (world == null ? "unknown zone" : world.zoneType.label), 3);
    }
```

Name: beginBuildPlacement
SHA256: 25054c742e702bbd11cd20c1f3f6d8e9fb9121f6d78db52fd1096cef5ad442a1

```java
    void beginBuildPlacement(BuildRecipe recipe) {
        if (recipe == null) return;
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Build planning failed: stand inside your claimed room first."); return; }
        String req = buildStructuralRequirementProblem(recipe);
        if (!req.equals("OK")) { logEvent("Build unavailable: " + recipe.name + " — " + req); return; }
        pendingBuildRecipe = recipe;
        buildPlacementActive = true;
        ConstructionPlacementFeedbackAuthority.invalidate();
        Point spot = findOpenBaseSpot();
        buildX = (spot == null ? playerX : spot.x);
        buildY = (spot == null ? playerY : spot.y);
        clampBuildCursorToClaimedRoom();
        updatePendingBuildSummary();
        if (universalWindowAuthority != null) universalWindowAuthority.open("construction", turn, "planning " + recipe.name);
        String governanceLine = constructionGovernanceAuthority.advisoryForBuild(constructionBlueprintFor(recipe), recipe.name, "begin build placement");
        DebugLog.audit("BUILD_PLAN", "recipe=" + recipe.name + " cursor=" + buildX + "," + buildY + " governance=" + governanceLine + " " + stateSummary());
        logEvent("Select a tile inside this claimed room for " + recipe.name + ". Use WASD/arrows, then press E to CONFIRM BUILD.");
        logEvent(governanceLine);
        repaint();
    }
```

Name: constructionPermissionRiskLine

```java
    String constructionPermissionRiskLine(BuildRecipe r) {
        if (r == null) return "unknown.";
        if (r.requiredFaction != Faction.NONE) return "restricted profile; expected affiliation is " + r.requiredFaction.label + ".";
        String low = r.name.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (r.attention >= 4 || low.contains("turret") || low.contains("sensor") || low.contains("security") || low.contains("shield")) return "high attention; security, gangs, or law may notice a fortified room.";
        if (low.contains("shop") || low.contains("business") || low.contains("clinic")) return "commercial attention; permits and local standing affect how lawful it looks.";
        if (low.contains("chem") || low.contains("distillation") || low.contains("fume") || low.contains("injector")) return "suspicious workshop profile; faction or law attention may rise around chemical work.";
        if (r.attention > 0) return "some attention; visible improvements can attract claims, raids, or inspection.";
        return "low attention; ordinary survival or storage construction.";
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1645-1663
Kind: method
Name: consumeBuildComponents
SHA256: 16eab14e84f777e9c1e6ab6401f852a18443935df543db6a1bc3ae63af14169c

```java
    boolean consumeBuildComponents(BuildRecipe r) {
        String problem = buildComponentRequirementProblem(r);
        if (!"OK".equals(problem)) { logEvent("Build blocked: " + problem); return false; }
        if (r == null || r.componentCosts.isEmpty()) return true;
        ArrayList<String> consumed = new ArrayList<>();
        for (Map.Entry<String,Integer> e : r.componentCosts.entrySet()) {
            for (int i=0; i<e.getValue(); i++) {
                ProductionInputConsumptionRecord rec = consumeProductionInputNamedResult(e.getKey(), "build component consumption for " + r.name);
                if (!rec.success) {
                    DebugLog.warn("BUILD_COMPONENT_RACE", "component vanished during build consume item=" + e.getKey() + " recipe=" + r.name + " state=" + stateSummary());
                    logEvent("Build interrupted: required component vanished from storage/inventory: " + e.getKey() + ".");
                    return false;
                }
                consumed.add(rec.shortLine());
            }
        }
        DebugLog.audit("BUILD_COMPONENTS_CONSUMED", "recipe=" + r.name + " components=" + consumed + " state=" + stateSummary());
        return true;
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1665-1695
Kind: method
Name: confirmBuildPlacement
SHA256: 05d7791ac9be43cd401198436124e118ae6d4654832b420e19b79d1303409f53

```java
    void confirmBuildPlacement() {
        if (!buildPlacementActive || pendingBuildRecipe == null) { logEvent("No build placement selected. Choose an object first."); return; }
        String req = buildStructuralRequirementProblem(pendingBuildRecipe);
        String place = canPlacePendingBuildAt(buildX, buildY);
        if (!req.equals("OK")) { if (universalWindowAuthority != null) universalWindowAuthority.open("construction", turn, req); logEvent("Build blocked: " + req); return; }
        if (!place.equals("OK")) { if (universalWindowAuthority != null) universalWindowAuthority.open("construction", turn, ConstructionPlacementFeedbackAuthority.universalWindowContext(place)); logEvent("Build blocked: " + ConstructionPlacementFeedbackAuthority.shortReason(place)); return; }
        int turnsNeeded = buildTurns(pendingBuildRecipe);
        int failChance = buildFailureChance(pendingBuildRecipe);
        gangHeat += pendingBuildRecipe.attention;
        suspicion += Math.max(0, pendingBuildRecipe.attention - 1);
        boolean failed = rng.nextInt(100) < failChance;
        if (failed) {
            logEvent("Construction planning failed: " + pendingBuildRecipe.name + ". No permanent site was placed. The machine-spirit rejects the geometry.");
            DebugLog.audit("BUILD_FAIL", "recipe=" + pendingBuildRecipe.name + " failChance=" + failChance + " turns=" + turnsNeeded + " cursor=" + buildX + "," + buildY + " " + stateSummary());
        } else {
            BaseObject site = ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.createSite(pendingBuildRecipe, buildX, buildY, turnsNeeded);
            site.description = pendingBuildRecipe.description + " Quality ceiling: " + site.qualityName + ". " + site.description;
            baseObjects.add(site);
            int inserted = ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.contribute(this, site, 1, true);
            logEvent("Placed staged construction site for " + pendingBuildRecipe.name + " at " + buildX + "," + buildY + ". Inserted components this action: " + inserted + ". " + ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.progressLine(site));
            String liveReady = LiveProductionPlacementAuthority.objectPlacementLine(this, site);
            if (liveReady != null && !liveReady.isBlank()) logEvent("PLACEMENT: " + liveReady);
            DebugLog.audit("STAGED_BUILD_SITE", "recipe=" + pendingBuildRecipe.name + " symbol=" + pendingBuildRecipe.symbol + " turns=" + turnsNeeded + " failChance=" + failChance + " cursor=" + buildX + "," + buildY + " blueprint=" + constructionBlueprintFor(pendingBuildRecipe) + " inserted=" + inserted + " progress=" + ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.progressLine(site) + " governance=" + constructionGovernanceAuthority.auditSummary() + " access=" + SelfEntombmentConstructionAuthority.auditSummary() + " feedback=" + ConstructionPlacementFeedbackAuthority.auditSummary() + " " + stateSummary());
        }
        advanceTurn("works on staged construction for " + pendingBuildRecipe.name + ".");
        pendingBuildRecipe = null;
        buildPlacementActive = false;
        pendingBuildSummary = "No build selected.";
        ConstructionPlacementFeedbackAuthority.invalidate();
        repaint();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1697-1708
Kind: method
Name: processProgressiveConstructionSites
SHA256: 833a744865c6242bc4544daa274bd4943aa11203f9f799f52364947487d0287b

```java
    void processProgressiveConstructionSites(boolean sleeping) {
        if (baseObjects == null || baseObjects.isEmpty()) return;
        int touched = 0;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) {
            if (obj != null && obj.underConstruction) {
                int before = obj.constructionVisualProgress;
                ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.contribute(this, obj, sleeping ? 2 : 0, true);
                if (obj.constructionVisualProgress != before) touched++;
            }
        }
        if (touched > 0 && turn % 10 == 0) DebugLog.audit("PROGRESSIVE_CONSTRUCTION_TICK", ProgressiveConstructionAuthority.auditSummary(this));
    }
```

SHA256: cd042defe21ae9317b4ce54015c2fbcb7da93951379eb7fc89b5703c3b6a4413

```java
    void buildBaseObject(String name, char symbol, int cost, int attention) {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Build failed: stand inside your claimed room first."); return; }
        if (supplies < cost) { logEvent("Build failed: " + name + " needs " + cost + " supplies; you have " + supplies + "."); return; }
        Point spot = findOpenBaseSpot();
        if (spot == null) { logEvent("Build failed: no open tile in claimed room for " + name + "."); return; }
        supplies -= cost;
        gangHeat += attention;
        suspicion += Math.max(0, attention - 1);
        BaseObject obj = new BaseObject(name, symbol, spot.x, spot.y, cost, attention);
        configureBaseObject(obj);
        baseObjects.add(obj);
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_BUILD", "built=" + obj.name + " symbol=" + symbol + " at=" + spot.x + "," + spot.y + " cost=" + cost + " attention=" + attention + " charges=" + obj.charges + " integrity=" + obj.integrity + " state=" + stateSummary());
        logEvent("Built " + name + " in claimed room. Supplies " + supplies + ". Attention rises because property implies value.");
        recordPlayerNewsEvent("facility-built", name, Faction.NONE, "base object built inside a claimed room", 2 + Math.max(0, attention));
    }
```

```java
    void passiveBaseObjectTicks() {
        hourlyNpcFactionProductionTick();
        if (!baseClaimed || baseObjects.isEmpty()) return;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) {
            if ((obj.symbol == 'u' || obj.symbol == 'e') && turn % (obj.symbol == 'e' ? 6 : 8) == 0 && obj.charges < obj.capacity) {
                obj.charges++;
                water = Math.min(MAX_FOOD_WATER, water + 1);
                DebugLog.audit("BASE_WATER_PASSIVE", obj.name + " gathered 1 water. water=" + water + " objectCharges=" + obj.charges + " state=" + stateSummary());
                logEvent("The water barrel knocks softly as condensation collects. Water reserve +1.");
            }
            if (obj.symbol == 'a' && obj.armed && turn % 10 == 0) {
                DebugLog.audit("BASE_ALARM_LISTEN", "Alarm trap remains armed at " + obj.x + "," + obj.y + " heat=" + gangHeat + " suspicion=" + suspicion);
            }
            if ((obj.symbol == 'T' || obj.symbol == 'H') && obj.armed && turn % TURNS_PER_HOUR == 0 && obj.charges < obj.capacity) {
                obj.charges++;
                DebugLog.audit("BASE_POWER_DEFENSE_CHARGE", obj.name + " charge=" + obj.charges + "/" + obj.capacity + " state=" + stateSummary());
            }
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1806-1828
Kind: method
Name: useComfortStructures
SHA256: 465e170d83cdd780810d3665c5783207524638168da1c24d2f769cc0271b2c16

```java
    void useComfortStructures() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Comfort structures require standing inside your claimed room."); return; }
        boolean did = false;
        BaseObject barrel = firstBaseObject('u');
        if (barrel != null && water > 0) {
            water--; barrel.charges = Math.max(0, barrel.charges - 1);
            fatigue = Math.max(0, fatigue - 2);
            did = true;
            logEvent("You drink from the water barrel. Fatigue -2. Water reserve " + water + ".");
            DebugLog.audit("BASE_USE_WATER", "water=" + water + " fatigue=" + fatigue + " state=" + stateSummary());
        }
        BaseObject cot = firstBaseObject('c');
        if (cot != null) {
            int oldFatigue = fatigue;
            fatigue = Math.max(0, fatigue - 4);
            if (wounds > 0 && water > 0) { wounds--; water--; logEvent("You rest on the cot and clean a wound. Wounds -1, water -1."); }
            else logEvent("You rest on the cot. Fatigue " + oldFatigue + " -> " + fatigue + ".");
            did = true;
            DebugLog.audit("BASE_USE_COT", "fatigue=" + fatigue + " wounds=" + wounds + " water=" + water + " state=" + stateSummary());
            advanceTurn("rests in a claimed room.");
        }
        if (!did) logEvent("No usable cot or filled water barrel is available yet.");
    }
```

```java
    void workProcessScrap() {
        if (!canUseWorkbench()) return;
        int scrapIndex = inventory.lastIndexOf("Scrap bit");
        if (scrapIndex < 0) { logEvent("Workbench: no Scrap bit available to process."); return; }
        removeInventoryAtWithTrace(scrapIndex);
        supplies += 2;
        machineParts += 1;
        fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + 1);
        BaseObject bench = firstBaseObject('w'); if (bench != null) bench.charges++;
        logEvent("Workbench processed scrap: +2 supplies, +1 machine part, fatigue +1.");
        ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordWorkbenchAction(this, firstBaseObject('w'), "process scrap", 1, active == null ? "player manual operation" : active.name + " manual operation");
        DebugLog.audit("WORKBENCH_PROCESS_SCRAP", "supplies=" + supplies + " parts=" + machineParts + " fatigue=" + fatigue + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("processes scrap at the workbench.");
    }
```

```java
    void workRepairClothing() {
        if (!canUseWorkbench()) return;
        if (equippedClothing == null || !equippedClothing.damaged) { logEvent("Workbench: equipped clothing is not damaged."); return; }
        if (supplies < 2 || machineParts < 1) { logEvent("Workbench: repairing clothing needs 2 supplies and 1 machine part."); return; }
        supplies -= 2; machineParts -= 1; equippedClothing.damaged = false;
        logEvent("Workbench repaired your damaged clothing. It may once again pass as deliberate misery.");
        ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordWorkbenchAction(this, firstBaseObject('w'), "repair clothing", 1, active == null ? "player manual operation" : active.name + " manual operation");
        DebugLog.audit("WORKBENCH_REPAIR_CLOTHING", "supplies=" + supplies + " parts=" + machineParts + " clothing=" + equippedClothing.name + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("repairs clothing at the workbench.");
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:1892-1916
Kind: method
Name: craftSelectedRecipe
SHA256: 6f4639dd74f28170ea10418857907dc45a13c4af15ee24a0649685b09e287ee0

```java
    void craftSelectedRecipe() {
        if (!canUseWorkbench()) return;
        java.util.List<CraftingRecipe> recipes = visibleCraftingRecipes();
        if (recipes.isEmpty()) { logEvent("Crafting blocked: no known recipes are available."); return; }
        CraftingRecipe r = recipes.get(Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedCraftRecipeIndex, recipes.size()-1)));
        if (r.disabled) { logEvent("Crafting blocked: no unlocked recipe is selected."); return; }
        String problem = r.blockingProblem(this);
        if (problem != null) { logEvent("Crafting blocked: " + problem); DebugLog.audit("CRAFT_BLOCKED", "recipe=" + r.name + " reason=" + problem + " state=" + stateSummary()); return; }
        BaseObject machine = requiredMachineFor(r);
        String q = cappedProductionQuality(machine, r.requiredKnowledge);
        Faction pf = productionFactionFor(machine, r.faction);
        ProductionRecipe pr = ProductionRecipe.create(r.outputBaseItem, pf, q, r.requiredKnowledge, machine == null ? "workbench" : machine.name);
        r.consumeInputs(this);
        int count = Math.max(1, r.outputCount + Math.max(0, pr.outputCharges()/4));
        for (int i=0;i<count;i++) addInventoryItem(pr.outputItemName(), ItemProvenanceRecord.produced(pr, machine, world, turn, active == null ? "player" : active.name));
        if (machine != null) { machine.charges = Math.min(machine.capacity, machine.charges + 1); machine.integrity = Math.max(1, machine.integrity - Math.max(0, r.machineWear)); }
        fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + r.fatigueCost);
        runCrafted += count;
        gainXp(r.xpSkill, r.xpGain, "crafting " + r.name);
        reportProductionCeiling(machine, pr);
        ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordManualRecipeCompletion(this, machine, r, Math.max(1, r.turnCost), count);
        logEvent("CRAFTED: " + count + "x " + pr.outputItemName() + " via " + r.name + ". Fatigue +" + r.fatigueCost + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("CRAFT_SUCCESS", r.auditLine() + " output=" + pr.outputItemName() + " count=" + count + " q=" + q + " machine=" + (machine==null?"none":machine.name) + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("crafts " + r.name + "."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void reportProductionCeiling(BaseObject obj, ProductionRecipe r) {
        int k = bestKnownProductionTier();
        int m = machineQualityTier(obj);
        if (m < k) logEvent("Production ceiling: " + obj.name + " is " + obj.qualityName + ", so output is capped at " + r.qualityName + ".");
        MachineTierProfile mp = MachineTierAuthority.forMachine(obj);
        DebugLog.audit("PRODUCTION_CEILING", "machine=" + (obj==null?"none":obj.name) + " machineQuality=" + (obj==null?"none":obj.qualityName) + " machineTier=" + m + " knowledgeTier=" + k + " outputQuality=" + r.qualityName + " machineProfile=" + mp.auditLine());
    }
```

```java
    void operateAtmosCondenser() {
        if (!canUseWorkbench()) return;

        if (condenser == null) { logEvent("Production blocked: no Atmospheric Condenser has been built in this base."); return; }
        if (!hasKnowledge("Condensation Handling")) { logEvent("Production blocked: Condensation Handling knowledge is required to run this recipe safely."); return; }
        String q = cappedProductionQuality(condenser, "Condensation Handling");
        Faction pf = productionFactionFor(condenser, Faction.HIVER);
```

```java
    void operateMicroForge() {
        if (!canUseWorkbench()) return;
        BaseObject forge = firstBaseObject('f');
        if (forge == null) { logEvent("Production blocked: no Micro Forge has been built in this base."); return; }
        if (!hasKnowledge("Scrap-Forging Doctrine")) { logEvent("Production blocked: Scrap-Forging Doctrine knowledge is required for this machine recipe."); return; }
        if (machineParts < 1) { logEvent("Production blocked: forging supplies needs 1 machine part."); return; }
        machineParts -= 1;
        String q = cappedProductionQuality(forge, "Scrap-Forging Doctrine");
        Faction pf = productionFactionFor(forge, Faction.MECHANIST_COLLEGIA);
        ProductionRecipe r = ProductionRecipe.create("Construction supplies", pf, q, "Scrap-Forging Doctrine", forge.name);
        supplies += r.outputCharges();
        addInventoryItem(r.outputItemName(), ItemProvenanceRecord.produced(r, forge, world, turn, active == null ? "player" : active.name));
        forge.charges++;
        fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + 1);
        gainXp("Mechanics", 3, "micro forge production");
        reportProductionCeiling(forge, r);
        logEvent("PRODUCTION: " + r.summary() + ". Build supplies +" + r.outputCharges() + ". Fatigue +1.");
        DebugLog.audit("PRODUCTION_FORGE", r.auditLine() + " supplies=" + supplies + " parts=" + machineParts + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("runs a micro forge recipe.");
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:2039-2057
Kind: method
Name: recruitActiveNpc
SHA256: 1edfb3d8cbd78707aaf2357299c9c1290ba37867cd8054fd0998a596e1dfd14d

```java
    void recruitActiveNpc() {
        if (activeConversationNpc == null) { logEvent("Recruitment failed: no active conversation target."); return; }
        if (!baseClaimed) { logEvent("Recruitment failed: claim a base before promising anyone a bunk and a tomorrow."); return; }
        if (!hasKnowledge("Recruit Berthing Doctrine")) { logEvent("Recruitment failed: Recruit Berthing Doctrine is required before faction housing can be organized."); return; }
        int cap = recruitCapacity();
        if (factionRecruits.size() >= cap) { logEvent("Recruitment failed: no free cot capacity. Built cots=" + cap + ", recruits=" + factionRecruits.size() + "."); return; }
        int standing = factionStanding.getOrDefault(activeConversationNpc.faction, 0);
        if (standing < -2) { logEvent("Recruitment failed: " + activeConversationNpc.faction.label + " standing is too poor for this person to trust your base."); return; }
        int cost = Math.max(1, 2 - Math.max(0, standing));
        if (supplies < cost) { logEvent("Recruitment failed: needs " + cost + " supplies as sign-on food, tools, and bunk kit. You have " + supplies + "."); return; }
        supplies -= cost;
        RecruitWorker rw = RecruitWorker.fromNpc(activeConversationNpc, factionRecruits.size()+1);
        factionRecruits.add(rw);
        if (world != null) world.npcs.remove(activeConversationNpc);
        logEvent("RECRUITED: " + rw.name + " joins your base as " + rw.role + ". Capacity " + factionRecruits.size() + "/" + recruitCapacity() + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("RECRUIT_SUCCESS", rw.saveLine() + " cost=" + cost + " capacity=" + recruitCapacity() + " state=" + stateSummary());
        activeConversationNpc = null; activeTrader = null;
        advanceTurn("recruits a faction worker.");
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:2221-2236

```java
    void assignSelectedRecipeToMachine() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Assignment failed: stand inside your claimed base room."); return; }
        if (!hasKnowledge("Workshop Labor Discipline")) { logEvent("Assignment failed: Workshop Labor Discipline is required before recruits can be assigned to machines."); return; }
        BaseObject machine = selectedWorkerMachine();
        if (machine == null) { logEvent("Assignment failed: no recruit-operable machine selected."); return; }
        java.util.List<CraftingRecipe> recipes = visibleCraftingRecipes();
        CraftingRecipe r = recipes.get(Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedCraftRecipeIndex, recipes.size()-1)));
        if (r.disabled) { logEvent("Assignment failed: no unlocked recipe selected."); return; }
        if (r.machineSymbol != ' ' && r.machineSymbol != machine.symbol) { logEvent("Assignment failed: " + r.name + " requires " + r.machineLabel() + ", not " + machine.name + "."); return; }
        String problem = r.assignmentProblem(this, machine);
        if (problem != null) { logEvent("Assignment failed: " + problem); return; }
        machine.assignedRecipe = r.name;
        machine.assignedWorker = factionRecruits.isEmpty() ? "unmanned" : factionRecruits.get(0).name;
        logEvent("ASSIGNED: " + machine.name + " will run " + r.name + " when recruits perform a production shift.");
        DebugLog.audit("RECIPE_ASSIGNED", "machine=" + machine.name + " recipe=" + r.name + " worker=" + machine.assignedWorker + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:2286-2297
Kind: method
Name: adjustSelectedMachineQueue
SHA256: 47c2f51f280ad34acdb9b4d763c18772b452b0c5cf1b4e7dccaaeef35ea3c8a1

```java
    void adjustSelectedMachineQueue(int delta) {
        BaseObject machine = selectedWorkerMachine();
        if (machine == null) { logEvent("Queue adjustment failed: no selected production machine or apparatus."); return; }
        machine.productionQueueTarget = Math.max(1, Math.min(12, machine.productionQueueTarget + delta));
        if (machine.assignedRecipe != null && !machine.assignedRecipe.isBlank()) machine.productionQueueRemaining = Math.max(1, Math.min(machine.productionQueueTarget, Math.max(machine.productionQueueRemaining, 1) + delta));
        FactionRecipeVariant v = machine.assignedRecipe == null ? null : ControlledProductionJobAuthority.findVariantByAssignmentKey(machine.assignedRecipe);
        String forecast = v == null ? "ordinary/empty queue target " + machine.productionQueueTarget : ControlledProductionJobAuthority.queueForecastLine(this, machine, v);
        lastGeneratedProductionQueueReport = forecast;
        logEvent("Production queue for " + machine.name + " set to target " + machine.productionQueueTarget + " run(s). " + forecast);
        DebugLog.audit("PRODUCTION_QUEUE_ADJUST", "machine=" + machine.name + " target=" + machine.productionQueueTarget + " remaining=" + machine.productionQueueRemaining + " forecast=" + forecast + " state=" + stateSummary());
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void assignSelectedGeneratedProductionJob() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Generated assignment failed: stand inside your claimed base room."); return; }
        BaseObject machine = selectedWorkerMachine();
        if (machine == null) { logEvent("Generated assignment failed: no recruit-operable machine or apparatus selected."); return; }
        FactionRecipeVariant v = selectedGeneratedProductionJob();
        if (v == null) { logEvent("Generated assignment failed: no generated production job is available under current filters."); return; }
        String problem = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.assignmentProblem(this, machine, v);
        if (problem != null) { logEvent("Generated assignment failed: " + problem); DebugLog.audit("GENERATED_ASSIGN_BLOCKED", "machine=" + machine.name + " job=" + v.outputName + " reason=" + problem + " state=" + stateSummary()); return; }
        machine.assignedRecipe = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.assignmentKey(v);
        machine.assignedWorker = availableRecruitLabor() > 0 ? firstAvailableRecruitName() : ControlledProductionJobAuthority.MANUAL_WORKER_LABEL;
        machine.productionQueueTarget = Math.max(1, machine.productionQueueTarget);
        machine.productionQueueRemaining = Math.max(1, machine.productionQueueTarget);
        lastGeneratedProductionReport = "Assigned " + v.outputName + " to " + machine.name + ". " + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.manualFallbackLine(this, machine, v);
        lastGeneratedProductionQueueReport = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.queueForecastLine(this, machine, v);
        logEvent("ASSIGNED GENERATED JOB: " + lastGeneratedProductionReport + " " + lastGeneratedProductionQueueReport);
        recordPlayerNewsEvent("production-started", v.outputName, v.faction, "production assigned to " + machine.name + " with queue " + machine.productionQueueRemaining + "/" + machine.productionQueueTarget, 3);
        DebugLog.audit("GENERATED_RECIPE_ASSIGNED", "machine=" + machine.name + " key=" + machine.assignedRecipe + " worker=" + machine.assignedWorker + " queueTarget=" + machine.productionQueueTarget + " queueRemaining=" + machine.productionQueueRemaining + " manualTurns=" + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.manualTurnCost(this, machine, v) + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void runManualSelectedProductionJob() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Manual operation failed: stand inside the claimed base room."); return; }
        BaseObject machine = selectedWorkerMachine();
        if (machine == null) { logEvent("Manual operation failed: no machine or apparatus selected."); return; }
        if (machine.assignedRecipe == null || machine.assignedRecipe.isBlank()) { logEvent("Manual operation failed: selected machine has no assigned recipe/job."); return; }
        if (ControlledProductionJobAuthority.isGeneratedAssignment(machine.assignedRecipe)) {
            FactionRecipeVariant v = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.findVariantByAssignmentKey(machine.assignedRecipe);
            if (v == null) { logEvent("Manual operation failed: assigned generated job is no longer available."); return; }
            if (machine.productionQueueRemaining <= 0) { logEvent("Manual operation blocked: assigned generated job queue is complete. Use QUEUE + or reassign the job to schedule more runs."); return; }
            String problem = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.operationProblem(this, machine, v, true);
            if (problem != null) { logEvent("Manual operation blocked: " + problem); DebugLog.audit("MANUAL_GENERATED_BLOCKED", "machine=" + machine.name + " job=" + v.outputName + " reason=" + problem + " state=" + stateSummary()); return; }
            runGeneratedProductionJob(machine, v, true);
            return;
        }
        CraftingRecipe r = CraftingRecipe.byName(machine.assignedRecipe);
        if (r == null) { logEvent("Manual operation failed: assigned recipe is no longer registered."); return; }
        String problem = r.blockingProblemForMachine(this, machine);
        if (problem != null) { logEvent("Manual operation blocked: " + problem); return; }
        String q = cappedProductionQuality(machine, r.requiredKnowledge);
        Faction pf = productionFactionFor(machine, r.faction);
        ProductionRecipe pr = ProductionRecipe.create(r.outputBaseItem, pf, q, r.requiredKnowledge, machine.name);
        r.consumeInputs(this);
        int count = Math.max(1, r.outputCount + Math.max(0, pr.outputCharges()/5));
        for (int i=0;i<count;i++) addBaseStorageItem(pr.outputItemName(), ItemProvenanceRecord.produced(pr, machine, world, turn, active == null ? "player manual operation" : active.name + " manual operation"));
        machine.charges = Math.min(Math.max(1, machine.capacity), machine.charges + 1);
        machine.integrity = Math.max(1, machine.integrity - Math.max(0, r.machineWear));
        int turnsNeeded = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.manualTurnCost(this, machine, r);
        fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.manualFatigueCost(this, machine, r));
        runCrafted += count;
        gainXp(r.xpSkill, Math.max(1, r.xpGain), "manual machine operation");
        reportProductionCeiling(machine, pr);
        ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordManualRecipeCompletion(this, machine, r, turnsNeeded, count);
        logEvent("MANUAL PRODUCTION: " + count + "x " + pr.outputItemName() + " produced into base storage by operating " + machine.name + " for " + turnsNeeded + " turns.");
        DebugLog.audit("MANUAL_RECIPE_PRODUCTION", "machine=" + machine.name + " recipe=" + r.name + " output=" + pr.outputItemName() + " count=" + count + " turns=" + turnsNeeded + " state=" + stateSummary());
        for (int i=0;i<turnsNeeded;i++) advanceTurn("operates " + machine.name + " manually.");
    }
```

```java
    void runGeneratedProductionJob(BaseObject machine, FactionRecipeVariant v, boolean manual) {
        if (machine == null || v == null) return;
        ProductionInputConsumptionRecord inputTrace = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.consumeInputsWithTrace(this, v, (manual ? "manual" : "crew") + " generated production for " + v.outputName);
        if (!inputTrace.success) {
            logEvent("Generated production aborted: " + inputTrace.failureReason);
            DebugLog.warn("GENERATED_INPUT_CONSUME_ABORT", "machine=" + machine.name + " variant=" + v.outputName + " reason=" + inputTrace.failureReason + " state=" + stateSummary());
            return;
        }
        FacilityOutputRunEstimate est = FacilityOutputModifierAuthority.estimate(this, machine, v, manual);
        String q = QualityAuthorityApi.cappedQualityName(v.requiredKnowledge, bestKnownProductionTier(), machineQualityTier(machine), QualityAuthorityApi.UNLIMITED_TIER, QualityAuthorityApi.UNLIMITED_TIER, QualityAuthorityApi.UNLIMITED_TIER);
        ProductionRecipe pr = ProductionRecipe.create(v.base.outputBaseItem, v.faction, q, v.requiredKnowledge, machine.name);
        int count = Math.max(1, est.outputCount);
        String operator = manual ? (active == null ? "player manual operation" : active.name + " manual operation") : (machine.assignedWorker == null || machine.assignedWorker.isBlank() ? "assigned recruit crew" : machine.assignedWorker);
        for (int i=0;i<count;i++) addBaseStorageItem(v.outputName, ItemProvenanceRecord.produced(pr, machine, world, turn, operator + " | " + est.shortLine() + " | inputs " + inputTrace.summaryLine()));
        machine.charges = Math.min(Math.max(1, machine.capacity), machine.charges + Math.max(1, est.queueThroughput));
        machine.integrity = Math.max(1, machine.integrity - Math.max(0, est.wear));
        if (est.breakdownRollPercent > 0 && rng.nextInt(100) < est.breakdownRollPercent) {
            int extraWear = Math.max(1, 1 + est.breakdownRollPercent / 18);
            machine.integrity = Math.max(1, machine.integrity - extraWear);
            logEvent("FACILITY STRAIN: " + machine.name + " suffers breakdown wear (" + extraWear + ") from " + v.outputName + ".");
            DebugLog.audit("FACILITY_BREAKDOWN_STRAIN", "machine=" + machine.name + " variant=" + v.outputName + " chance=" + est.breakdownRollPercent + " extraWear=" + extraWear + " integrity=" + machine.integrity + " state=" + stateSummary());
        }
        runCrafted += count;
        applyFactionMarketPressureFromGeneratedProduction(v, count);
        int xpGain = Math.max(1, manual ? 3 : Math.max(1, est.workerCapacityUsed));
        gainXp(ControlledProductionJobAuthority.skillFor(v), xpGain, manual ? "manual generated production" : "recruit generated production");
        reportProductionCeiling(machine, pr);
        int turnsNeeded = Math.max(1, est.turns);
        if (manual) fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.manualFatigueCost(this, machine, v));
        if (machine.productionQueueRemaining > 0) machine.productionQueueRemaining = Math.max(0, machine.productionQueueRemaining - Math.max(1, est.queueThroughput));
        String queueTail = " Queue remaining " + machine.productionQueueRemaining + "/" + Math.max(1, machine.productionQueueTarget) + ".";
        String modTail = " Facility modifiers: " + est.shortLine() + ".";
        ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordGeneratedCompletion(this, machine, v, manual, turnsNeeded, count, operator);
        if (manual) logEvent("MANUAL GENERATED PRODUCTION: " + count + "x " + v.outputName + " produced into base storage. Time " + turnsNeeded + " turns; fatigue +" + ControlledProductionJobAuthority.manualFatigueCost(this, machine, v) + "." + queueTail + modTail);
        else logEvent("CREW GENERATED PRODUCTION: " + count + "x " + v.outputName + " produced into base storage by " + operator + "." + queueTail + modTail);
        if (machine.productionQueueRemaining <= 0) DebugLog.audit("PRODUCTION_QUEUE_COMPLETE", "machine=" + machine.name + " variant=" + v.outputName + " target=" + machine.productionQueueTarget + " state=" + stateSummary());
        DebugLog.audit(manual ? "MANUAL_GENERATED_PRODUCTION" : "RECRUIT_GENERATED_PRODUCTION", "machine=" + machine.name + " variant=" + v.outputName + " count=" + count + " turns=" + turnsNeeded + " wear=" + est.wear + " breakdownChance=" + est.breakdownRollPercent + " operator=" + operator + " queueRemaining=" + machine.productionQueueRemaining + " modifiers=" + est.shortLine() + " inputs=" + inputTrace.summaryLine() + " law=" + v.lawStatus + " state=" + stateSummary());
        for (int i=0;i<turnsNeeded;i++) advanceTurn((manual ? "manually operates " : "supervises ") + machine.name + ".");
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard5.txt:2412-2420

Name: applyFactionMarketPressureFromGeneratedProduction
SHA256: 4bdd92125cd4e6e73ac0947873933d10c37ac053bd4eb65484d149be0aa414bf

```java
    void applyFactionMarketPressureFromGeneratedProduction(FactionRecipeVariant v, int count) {
        if (v == null) return;
        int pressure = Math.max(0, count);
        if (v.lawStatus != null && (v.lawStatus.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("illegal") || v.lawStatus.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("contraband") || v.lawStatus.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("seizure"))) {
            gangHeat += Math.max(1, pressure);
            suspicion += Math.max(1, pressure/2);
        }
        factionMarketPressure.put(v.faction, factionMarketPressure.getOrDefault(v.faction,0) + pressure);
    }
```

```java
    void runRecruitProductionShift() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Crew shift failed: stand inside the claimed base room."); return; }
        if (!hasKnowledge("Workshop Labor Discipline")) { logEvent("Crew shift failed: Workshop Labor Discipline is required for recruit-operated production."); return; }
        if (factionRecruits.isEmpty()) { logEvent("Crew shift has no recruited workers. Select an assigned machine and use MANUAL RUN to operate it yourself with a time cost."); return; }
        int labor = availableRecruitLabor();
        int done = 0;
        ArrayList<String> outputs = new ArrayList<>();
        for (BaseObject machine : recruitOperableMachines()) {
            if (labor <= 0) break;
            if (machine.assignedRecipe == null || machine.assignedRecipe.isBlank()) continue;
            if (ControlledProductionJobAuthority.isGeneratedAssignment(machine.assignedRecipe)) {
                FactionRecipeVariant v = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.findVariantByAssignmentKey(machine.assignedRecipe);
                if (v == null) { logEvent("Crew shift skipped " + machine.name + ": assigned generated job is no longer registered."); continue; }
                if (machine.productionQueueRemaining <= 0) { logEvent("Crew shift skipped " + v.outputName + ": queue complete on " + machine.name + ". Use QUEUE + or reassign to schedule more runs."); continue; }
                String problem = ControlledProductionJobAuthority.operationProblem(this, machine, v, false);
                if (problem != null) { logEvent("Crew shift skipped " + v.outputName + ": " + problem + ". Manual fallback remains available when the player operates the selected machine."); continue; }
                runGeneratedProductionJob(machine, v, false);
                outputs.add(v.outputName);
                done++; labor--;
                continue;
            }
            CraftingRecipe r = CraftingRecipe.byName(machine.assignedRecipe);
            if (r == null) { logEvent("Crew shift skipped " + machine.name + ": assigned recipe is no longer registered."); continue; }
            String problem = r.blockingProblemForMachine(this, machine);
            if (problem != null) { logEvent("Crew shift skipped " + r.name + ": " + problem); continue; }
            String q = cappedProductionQuality(machine, r.requiredKnowledge);
            Faction pf = productionFactionFor(machine, r.faction);
            ProductionRecipe pr = ProductionRecipe.create(r.outputBaseItem, pf, q, r.requiredKnowledge, machine.name);
            r.consumeInputs(this);
            int count = Math.max(1, r.outputCount + Math.max(0, pr.outputCharges()/5));
            for (int i=0;i<count;i++) addBaseStorageItem(pr.outputItemName(), ItemProvenanceRecord.produced(pr, machine, world, turn, machine.assignedWorker == null || machine.assignedWorker.isBlank() ? "assigned recruit crew" : machine.assignedWorker));
            machine.charges = Math.min(Math.max(1, machine.capacity), machine.charges + 1);
            machine.integrity = Math.max(1, machine.integrity - Math.max(0, r.machineWear));
            applyFactionMarketPressureFromProduction(r, pr, count);
            outputs.add(count + "x " + pr.outputItemName());
            done++; labor--;
            gainXp(r.xpSkill, Math.max(1, r.xpGain/2), "supervising recruit production");
            reportProductionCeiling(machine, pr);
            ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordRecruitRecipeCompletion(this, machine, r, 1, count, machine.assignedWorker == null || machine.assignedWorker.isBlank() ? "assigned recruit crew" : machine.assignedWorker);
            DebugLog.audit("RECRUIT_PRODUCTION", "machine=" + machine.name + " recipe=" + r.name + " output=" + pr.outputItemName() + " count=" + count + " state=" + stateSummary());
        }
        if (done == 0) { logEvent("Crew shift produced nothing: assign recipes to machines and ensure inputs are available."); return; }
        fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + 1);
        logEvent("CREW SHIFT: " + done + " machine(s) produced into base storage: " + String.join("; ", outputs) + ".");
        advanceTurn("supervises a recruit production shift.");
    }
```

```java
    void useWorkshopStructures() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Workshop use requires standing inside your claimed room."); return; }
        BaseObject bench = firstBaseObject('w');
        if (bench == null) { logEvent("No scrap workbench built yet."); return; }
        int scrapIndex = inventory.lastIndexOf("Scrap bit");
        if (scrapIndex >= 0) {
            removeInventoryAtWithTrace(scrapIndex);
            supplies += 2;
            machineParts += 1;
            fatigue = Math.min(20, fatigue + 1);
            bench.charges++;
            logEvent("You process scrap at the workbench: +2 supplies, +1 machine part, fatigue +1.");
            ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordWorkbenchAction(this, bench, "process scrap", 1, active == null ? "player manual operation" : active.name + " manual operation");
            DebugLog.audit("BASE_WORKBENCH_SCRAP", "supplies=" + supplies + " parts=" + machineParts + " fatigue=" + fatigue + " benchUses=" + bench.charges + " state=" + stateSummary());
            advanceTurn("works at the scrap bench.");
            return;
        }
        if (equippedClothing != null && equippedClothing.damaged && supplies >= 2 && machineParts >= 1) {
            supplies -= 2; machineParts -= 1; equippedClothing.damaged = false;
            logEvent("You repair your damaged clothing at the workbench. It may once again pass as intentional poverty.");
            ProductionQueueRecordBridge.recordWorkbenchAction(this, bench, "repair clothing", 1, active == null ? "player manual operation" : active.name + " manual operation");
            DebugLog.audit("BASE_WORKBENCH_REPAIR_CLOTHING", "supplies=" + supplies + " parts=" + machineParts + " clothing=" + equippedClothing.name + " state=" + stateSummary());
            advanceTurn("repairs clothing.");
            return;
        }
        logEvent("Workbench idle: bring Scrap bit, damaged clothing, supplies, or machine parts for useful work.");
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_WORKBENCH_IDLE", "inventory=" + inventory.size() + " supplies=" + supplies + " parts=" + machineParts + " clothingDamaged=" + (equippedClothing!=null && equippedClothing.damaged));
    }
```

```java
    void useSecurityStructures() {
        if (!baseClaimed || !isInClaimedRoom(playerX, playerY)) { logEvent("Security structures require standing inside your claimed room."); return; }
        int barricades = 0, cover = 0, armed = 0, posts = 0, barracks = 0, doors = 0, turrets = 0, shields = 0;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) {
            if (obj.symbol == 'd') { barricades++; cover += obj.cover; }
            if (obj.symbol == 'a') { obj.armed = true; armed++; }
            if (obj.symbol == 'p') { posts++; cover += obj.cover; }
            if (obj.symbol == 'g') { barracks++; cover += obj.cover; }
            if (obj.symbol == 'D') { doors++; cover += obj.cover; }
            if (obj.symbol == 'T') { turrets++; cover += obj.cover; obj.armed = true; }
            if (obj.symbol == 'H') { shields++; cover += obj.cover; obj.armed = true; }
        }
        int deterrence = baseSecurityRating();
        logEvent("Security checked: barricades=" + barricades + ", watch posts=" + posts + ", guard barracks=" + barracks + ", reinforced doors=" + doors + ", powered turrets=" + turrets + ", shield relays=" + shields + ", armed alarms=" + armed + ", guards=" + securityStaffCount() + ", defense rating=" + deterrence + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_SECURITY_CHECK", "barricades=" + barricades + " posts=" + posts + " barracks=" + barracks + " doors=" + doors + " armed=" + armed + " guards=" + securityStaffCount() + " rating=" + deterrence + " heat=" + gangHeat + " suspicion=" + suspicion + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```
