```java
    void interactBaseObject(BaseObject obj) {
        if (obj != null && obj.underConstruction) {
            contributeToConstructionSite(obj);
            return;
        }
        String passiveDefenseLine = PassiveDefenseEffectsAuthority.isPassiveDefense(obj.symbol) ? PassiveDefenseEffectsAuthority.inspectLine(obj) : null;
        switch (obj.symbol) {
            case 's': logEvent("Storage crate accessed. Capacity " + obj.capacity + ". Base storage currently " + baseStorage.size() + " item(s). Use STASH/TAKE."); break;
            case 'w': logEvent("Scrap workbench accessed. Uses=" + obj.charges + ". Converts Scrap bit into supplies/parts and repairs damaged clothing."); break;
            case 'd': logEvent("Barricade inspected. " + passiveDefenseLine); break;
            case 'S': case 'R': case 'W': case 'D': case 'Y': case 'N': case 'P': case 'J': case 'U': case 'Z': case 'T': case 'H': logEvent("Defense inspected. " + passiveDefenseLine); break;
            case 'c': logEvent("Sleeping cot inspected. Use DRINK/REST to reduce fatigue and later recover wounds/body damage."); break;
            case 'u': logEvent("Water barrel inspected. Stored water charges " + obj.charges + "/" + obj.capacity + ". Global reserve " + water + "."); break;
            case 'a': logEvent("Alarm trap inspected. Armed=" + obj.armed + ". Use SECURITY to arm it and audit base defenses."); break;
            default: logEvent("Base object inspected: " + obj.name + ". " + obj.description + (passiveDefenseLine == null ? "" : " " + passiveDefenseLine));
        }
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_OBJECT_INSPECT", obj.name + " symbol=" + obj.symbol + " integrity=" + obj.integrity + " charges=" + obj.charges + " armed=" + obj.armed + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void spawnBountyTarget(FactionContract c) {
        if (world == null) return;
        for (NpcEntity n : world.npcs) if (c.targetEntityId.equals(n.id)) return;
        Point p = world.randomOpenPoint(rng);
        if (p == null) p = world.startPoint();
        Faction hostile = rivalFactionForContract(c.faction);
        NpcEntity n = NpcEntity.create(hostile, world.zoneType, p.x, p.y, rng);
        n.id = c.targetEntityId;
        n.name = c.targetName;
        n.role = "Contract Bounty Target";
        n.state = "Hostile";
        n.hp = 16 + Math.max(0, factionStanding.getOrDefault(c.faction,0));
        world.npcs.add(n);
        c.spawned = true;
        logEvent("CONTRACT TARGET SPAWNED: " + n.name + " is somewhere in this zone. Retrieve " + c.publicRequiredItem() + " from the body.");
        DebugLog.audit("CONTRACT_SPAWN_BOUNTY", c.longLine() + " at " + p.x + "," + p.y + " zone=" + keySafe(c.targetZoneKey));
    }
```

```java
    void spawnFetchObject(FactionContract c) {
```

```java
    void readFactionJournalAt(int tx, int ty) {
        MapObjectState m = factionJournalObjectAt(tx, ty);
        if (m == null) { logEvent("FACTION JOURNAL: no readable journal here."); return; }
        FactionStrategicPlan p = findFactionStrategicPlanById(m.stockState);
        if (p == null) { logEvent("FACTION JOURNAL: " + m.label + " exists, but the indexed plan has been lost or moved."); return; }
        logEvent("FACTION JOURNAL: " + p.journalHeader());
        logEvent("  Immediate: " + p.immediateGoal + " / phase " + p.phase + " until turn " + p.phaseUntilTurn + ".");
        logEvent("  Long term: " + p.longTermGoal + ". Personal goal: " + p.personalGoal + ".");
        if (p.scheme != null && !p.scheme.isBlank()) logEvent("  Scheme: " + p.scheme + " involving " + p.schemeTargetFaction.label + ".");
        if (p.lastOutcome != null && !p.lastOutcome.isBlank()) logEvent("  Last outcome: " + p.lastOutcome);
        if (p.history != null && !p.history.isEmpty()) {
            int start = Math.max(0, p.history.size() - 5);
            for (int i=start; i<p.history.size(); i++) logEvent("  Journal entry: " + p.history.get(i));
        }
        DebugLog.audit("FACTION_JOURNAL_READ", "plan=" + p.id + " faction=" + p.faction + " at=" + tx + "," + ty + " turn=" + turn);
    }
```

```java
    void stealFactionJournalAt(int tx, int ty) {
        MapObjectState m = factionJournalObjectAt(tx, ty);
        if (m == null) { logEvent("STEAL JOURNAL: no faction journal is selected."); return; }
        FactionStrategicPlan p = findFactionStrategicPlanById(m.stockState);
        if (p == null) { logEvent("STEAL JOURNAL: journal exists, but the plan ledger reference is missing."); return; }
        if (inventoryWeight() + 1 > carryCapacity()) { logEvent("STEAL JOURNAL blocked: carrying load is full."); return; }
        String item = stolenJournalItemName(p);
        addInventoryItem(item, ItemProvenanceRecord.of(item, p.faction, p.leaderName + " private room", world, turn, "leader journal: " + p.shortLine(), "stolen from faction leader journal object"));
        world.mapObjects.remove(m);
        if (world.inBounds(tx,ty)) world.tiles[tx][ty] = '.';
        logEvent("STEAL JOURNAL: lifted " + item + ". INN bounty estimate " + InnBountyApi.journalBounty(item, p) + " Concord Script if sold to the press.");
        DebugLog.audit("FACTION_JOURNAL_STOLEN", "plan=" + p.id + " faction=" + p.faction + " item=" + item + " at=" + tx + "," + ty + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("steals a faction leader journal.");
        updatePendingInteractionSummary(); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void sellLeaderJournalsToINN() {
        if (!canSellLeaderJournalsToINNAt(lookX, lookY)) { logEvent("INN BOUNTY: sell stolen faction journals at an INN bureau or newspaper dispenser contact point."); return; }
        int sold = 0, paid = 0;
        for (int i=inventory.size()-1; i>=0; i--) {

            int bounty = InnBountyApi.journalBounty(item, null);
            removeInventoryAtWithTrace(i);
            addImperialScript(bounty);
            sold++; paid += bounty;
        }
        if (sold <= 0) { logEvent("INN BOUNTY: no stolen faction leader journals carried. Editors cannot pay for paranoia without paperwork."); return; }
        logEvent("INN BOUNTY: sold " + sold + " stolen leader journal(s) for " + paid + " Concord Script. The editor smiles like a guillotine learning to read.");
        DebugLog.audit("INN_JOURNAL_BOUNTY", "sold=" + sold + " paid=" + paid + " cash=" + countMoney() + " state=" + stateSummary());
```

```java
    void depositToSelectedBank(int amount) {
```

```java
    void withdrawFromSelectedBank(int amount) {
        BankProfile b = selectedBankProfile();
        if (b == null) { logEvent("BANK: no bank selected."); return; }
        if (!openBankAccounts.contains(b.id)) { logEvent("BANK: no open account at " + b.label + "."); return; }
        int bal = bankBalance(b.id);
        if (bal <= 0) { logEvent("BANK: account at " + b.label + " is empty."); return; }
        int n = Math.min(bal, amount == Integer.MAX_VALUE ? bal : Math.max(0, amount));
        if (n <= 0) { logEvent("BANK: withdrawal amount must be positive."); return; }
        int fee = Math.min(n, selectedBankTerminalKind().contains("kiosk") ? b.kioskFee : b.branchFee);
        int delivered = Math.max(0, n - fee);
        bankBalances.put(b.id, bal - n);
        addImperialScript(delivered);
        lastBankReport = "Withdrew " + delivered + " script from " + b.label + " after fee " + fee + ".";
        logEvent("BANK: withdrew " + delivered + " Concord Script from " + b.label + " (fee " + fee + "). Balance now " + bankBalance(b.id) + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("BANK_WITHDRAW", "bank=" + b.id + " gross=" + n + " fee=" + fee + " delivered=" + delivered + " balance=" + bankBalance(b.id) + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("withdraws bank cash."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void openBankVaultAt(int tx, int ty) {
        MapObjectState m = bankVaultAt(tx, ty);
        if (m == null) { logEvent("BANK VAULT: no vault selected."); return; }
        BankProfile b = bankProfileFromStock(m.stockState);
        if (bankVaultLooted(m)) { logEvent("BANK VAULT: " + b.label + " vault has already been emptied. The remaining wealth is structural arrogance."); return; }
        int access = bankVaultAccessScore();
        int diff = bankVaultDifficulty(b);
        boolean credential = countInventory("Bank manager keycard") > 0 || countInventory("Secure vault key") > 0;
        boolean localAlarmDisabled = nearbyBankAlarmPanelDisabled(tx, ty, b);
        int roll = rng.nextInt(100);
        if (!credential && access + roll < diff) {
            int sev = Math.max(3, diff/18);
            if (localAlarmDisabled) sev = Math.max(1, sev - 2);
            raiseBankHeistAlarmAt(b, "failed vault access roll " + (access + roll) + " vs " + diff, sev, tx, ty);
            if (m.stockState != null && !m.stockState.contains("alarmed=true")) m.stockState += ";alarmed=true";
            logEvent("BANK VAULT FAILED: access score " + access + "+roll " + roll + " < difficulty " + diff + ". Alarm pressure rises. " + lastBankHeistReport);
            advanceTurn("fails a bank vault intrusion."); repaint(); return;
        }
        ArrayList<String> loot = BankHeistApi.vaultLootFor(b, rng);
        int cash = BankHeistApi.vaultCashFor(b, rng);
        for (String item : loot) addInventoryItem(item, ItemProvenanceRecord.of(item, Faction.NOBLE, b.label + " vault", world, turn, "vault reserve / client sealed property", "stolen from bank vault by player"));
        addImperialScript(cash);
        m.vendCount = 1;
        if (m.stockState == null) m.stockState = b.id;
        if (!m.stockState.contains("locked=false")) m.stockState += ";locked=false";
        if (!m.stockState.contains("open=true")) m.stockState += ";open=true";
        if (!m.stockState.contains("looted=true")) m.stockState += ";looted=true";
        lootedBankVaultIds.add(m.id);
        suspicion += b.upperHive ? 8 : (b.midHive ? 5 : 3);
        gangHeat += 1;
        lastBankHeistReport = "Opened " + b.label + " vault at " + (world == null ? "unknown zone" : world.zoneName) + "; stole " + loot.size() + " item(s) and " + cash + " script; suspicion now " + suspicion + ".";
        logEvent("BANK HEIST: " + lastBankHeistReport + " Loot: " + String.join(", ", loot) + ".");
        recordPlayerNewsEvent("bank-heist", b.label + " vault breach", Faction.NOBLE, "unreported vault breach at " + b.label + "; authorities are comparing permits, keys, and shoeprints", Math.max(5, loot.size()+3));
        int alarmSeverity = Math.max(5, loot.size()+2);
        if (localAlarmDisabled) alarmSeverity = Math.max(2, alarmSeverity - 3);
        raiseBankHeistAlarmAt(b, localAlarmDisabled ? "vault opened after alarm panel bypass" : "vault opened", alarmSeverity, tx, ty);
        DebugLog.audit("BANK_VAULT_OPEN", "bank=" + b.id + " items=" + loot + " cash=" + cash + " score=" + access + " diff=" + diff + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("loots a bank vault."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void stealBankManagerKeycardAt(int tx, int ty) {

        if (n == null) { logEvent("KEYCARD THEFT: no bank manager selected."); return; }
        if (countInventory("Bank manager keycard") > 0) { logEvent("KEYCARD THEFT: you already carry a bank manager keycard. Multiple felonies do not make the first one tidier."); return; }
```

```java
    void raiseBankHeistAlarmAt(BankProfile b, String reason, int severity, int tx, int ty) {
        int sev = Math.max(1, severity);
        bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn, turn + (2 + sev) * TURNS_PER_HOUR);
        authorityFacilityInspectionCooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(authorityFacilityInspectionCooldownUntilTurn, turn + Math.max(2, sev) * TURNS_PER_HOUR);
        suspicion += Math.max(1, sev);
        if (b != null && b.upperHive) suspicion += 2;
        lastBankHeistReport = "Bank alarm pressure: " + (b==null?"unknown bank":b.label) + " / " + reason + " / severity " + sev + "; alarm cooldown until turn " + bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn + ".";
        lastBankAlarmReport = lastBankHeistReport;
        if (world != null) {
            for (MapObjectState m : world.mapObjects) {
                if (m == null || !"bank-alarm-panel".equals(m.type)) continue;
                if (Math.abs(m.x - tx) + Math.abs(m.y - ty) > 12 + sev) continue;
                if (m.stockState != null && !m.stockState.contains("alarmed=true")) m.stockState += ";alarmed=true";
                m.cooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(m.cooldownUntilTurn, bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn);
            }
        }
        alertBankGuardsNear(tx, ty, b, sev);
        DebugLog.audit("BANK_HEIST_ALARM", "bank=" + (b==null?"unknown":b.id) + " reason=" + reason + " severity=" + sev + " cooldown=" + bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn + " at=" + tx + "," + ty + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void tamperBankAlarmPanelAt(int tx, int ty) {
        MapObjectState m = bankAlarmPanelAt(tx, ty);
        if (m == null) { logEvent("BANK ALARM: no alarm panel selected."); return; }
        if (bankAlarmPanelDisabled(m)) { logEvent("BANK ALARM: this panel is already disabled or sufficiently pacified."); return; }
        BankProfile b = bankProfileFromStock(m.stockState);
        int score = stat("Intellect", 6) * 5 + stat("Agility", 6) * 3;
        if (countInventory("Data spike") > 0) score += 22;
        if (countInventory("Lockpicks") > 0) score += 8;
        if (countInventory("Hacking tools") > 0 || countInventory("Tool bundle") > 0 || countInventory("Mechanist Collegia tool roll") > 0) score += 16;
        if ("SNEAK".equals(movementModeLabel()) || "SNEAK".equals(activeMotionStateLabel())) score += 10;
        int diff = b == null ? 60 : (b.upperHive ? 105 : (b.midHive ? 82 : 58));
        int roll = rng.nextInt(100);
        if (score + roll >= diff) {
            if (m.stockState == null) m.stockState = b.id;
            if (!m.stockState.contains("disabled=true")) m.stockState += ";disabled=true";
            disabledBankAlarmPanelIds.add(m.id);
            bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(turn, Math.min(bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn, turn + TURNS_PER_HOUR));
            lastBankAlarmReport = "Disabled " + b.label + " branch alarm panel at " + tx + "," + ty + "; vault alarm response is reduced until maintenance notices.";
            logEvent("BANK ALARM TAMPER: " + lastBankAlarmReport);
            gainXp("Stealth", 2, "silenced a bank alarm panel");
            gainXp("Tech", 1, "bypassed bank alarm logic");
            DebugLog.audit("BANK_ALARM_PANEL_DISABLED", "bank=" + b.id + " score=" + score + " roll=" + roll + " diff=" + diff + " state=" + stateSummary());
        } else {
            suspicion += 4; gangHeat += 1; m.cooldownUntilTurn = Math.max(m.cooldownUntilTurn, turn + 3 * TURNS_PER_HOUR);
            raiseBankHeistAlarm(b, "failed alarm-panel tamper at " + tx + "," + ty, 5);
            lastBankAlarmReport = "Failed to disable " + b.label + " branch alarm panel; the box screamed to every clerk, guard, and ledger within administrative distance.";
            logEvent("BANK ALARM TAMPER FAILED: " + lastBankAlarmReport);
            DebugLog.audit("BANK_ALARM_PANEL_FAIL", "bank=" + b.id + " score=" + score + " roll=" + roll + " diff=" + diff + " state=" + stateSummary());
        }
        advanceTurn("tampers with a bank alarm panel."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void applyBankManagerSchedules() {
        if (world == null || turn % Math.max(1, TURNS_PER_HOUR/2) != 0) return;
        for (NpcEntity n : world.npcs) {
            if (!isBankManager(n)) continue;
            int phase = Math.floorMod(turn / Math.max(1, TURNS_PER_HOUR), 4);
            if (phase == 0) n.state = "Vault Desk";
            else if (phase == 1) n.state = "Counting Script";
            else if (phase == 2) n.state = "Inspecting Vault";
            else n.state = "Reviewing Lockboxes";
        }
    }
```

```java
    void applyBankAlarmPressureTick() {
        if (world == null || turn >= bankHeistAlarmCooldownUntilTurn) return;
        if (turn % Math.max(1, TURNS_PER_HOUR/2) != 0) return;
        int alerted = 0;
        for (NpcEntity n : world.npcs) {
            if (n == null || n.role == null) continue;
            String role = n.role.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if (role.contains("bank security") || role.contains("vault guard") || role.contains("branch guard")) {
                if (!"Alarm Response".equals(n.state)) { n.state = "Alarm Response"; alerted++; }
                n.activeMotionStateIndex = MOTION_RUN;
            }
        }
        if (alerted > 0) {
            lastBankAlarmReport = "Bank alarm is still active; " + alerted + " branch guard(s) have shifted into alarm response.";
            logEvent("BANK SECURITY: " + lastBankAlarmReport);
        }
    }
```

```java
    void turnInBankLockboxContract() {
        FactionContract found = null;
        for (FactionContract c : factionContracts) if (!c.completed && "LOCKBOX".equals(c.type)) { found = c; break; }
        if (found == null) { logEvent("LOCKBOX CONTRACT: no active noble-bank retrieval job is open."); return; }
        if (!inventory.contains(found.requiredTurnInItem)) { logEvent("LOCKBOX CONTRACT: you need " + found.publicRequiredItem() + " for the active noble retrieval job. Current report: " + lastBankLockboxContractReport); return; }

        found.completed = true;
        addImperialScript(found.payout);
        factionStanding.put(Faction.NOBLE, factionStanding.getOrDefault(Faction.NOBLE, 0) + found.repReward);
        suspicion += Math.max(1, found.payout / 800);
        lastBankLockboxContractReport = "Completed the noble retrieval job by delivering " + found.publicRequiredItem() + "; paid " + found.payout + " script and gained noble standing +" + found.repReward + ".";
```

```java
    void inspectSelectedPersistentStockObject() {
        MapObjectState m = persistentStockObjectAt(lookX, lookY);
        if (m == null) { logEvent("PERSISTENT STOCK INSPECTION: no contract or corpse container selected."); return; }
        String cid = persistentContainerIdForObject(m);
        ContainerRecord c = itemContainers.get(cid);
        logEvent("PERSISTENT STOCK: " + m.label + " / " + cid + " / items " + (c == null ? 0 : c.itemInstanceIds.size()) + ".");
        if (m.vendCount > 0) logEvent("PERSISTENT STOCK: corpse still has " + m.vendCount + " concord script recoverable on search.");
        if (c == null || c.itemInstanceIds.isEmpty()) { logEvent("PERSISTENT STOCK: container is empty; confirm/take-all will clear the abandoned marker."); return; }
        int shown = 0;
        for (String id : c.itemInstanceIds) {
            ItemInstance inst = itemInstances.get(id);
            if (inst == null) logEvent("  - " + id + " MISSING REGISTRY ENTRY");
            else logEvent("  - " + inst.displayName + " [" + id + "] " + (inst.provenance == null ? "untraced" : inst.provenance.summary()));
            if (++shown >= 5) { if (c.itemInstanceIds.size() > shown) logEvent("  ... " + (c.itemInstanceIds.size() - shown) + " more item(s)."); break; }
        }
        DebugLog.audit("PERSISTENT_STOCK_INSPECT", "object=" + m.id + " container=" + cid + " items=" + c.itemInstanceIds.size() + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

SHA256: 46d0aa3001be9085cc83f44d42eb4f32a86bcf0bc2bbd105d799ecd14755ed0b

```java
    String createCorpseLootContainer(NpcEntity target, String cause) {
        if (world == null || target == null) return "No corpse container created.";
        String corpseId = "CORPSE-" + ContainerIdentityApi.safeToken(target.id == null ? target.name : target.id) + "-" + Math.abs(Objects.hash(turn, target.x, target.y));
        String cid = corpseLootContainerId(corpseId);
        ensureContainer(cid, "Corpse loot: " + target.name);

        LootDropSystemAuthority.LootResolution resolved = LootDropSystemAuthority.resolveEntityDeathLoot(
                LootDropSystemAuthority.npcInventory(target),
                world.zoneType,
                LootDropSystemAuthority.sectorZoneTier(world),
                target.x, target.y, rng, cause);

        ArrayList<String> corpseLoot = new ArrayList<>(resolved.corpseItemNames());
        for (FactionContract c : factionContracts) {
            if (!c.completed && c.type.equals("BOUNTY") && c.targetEntityId.equals(target.id)) {
                corpseLoot.add(c.requiredTurnInItem);
                c.spawned = false;
            }
        }
        if (corpseLoot.isEmpty() && resolved.groundItemNames().isEmpty() && resolved.imperialScript() <= 0) {
            ArrayList<String> legacyFallback = corpseLootFor(target);
            if (!legacyFallback.isEmpty()) corpseLoot.add(legacyFallback.get(0));
        }
        addLootListToContainer(cid, "Corpse loot: " + target.name, corpseLoot, target.faction, "body of " + target.name, "corpse inventory after " + cause, "persistent corpse loot container");

        MapObjectState m = MapObjectState.corpseObject(target.x, target.y, corpseId, "Corpse of " + target.name, cid, target.faction, world.zoneType);
        m.vendCount = resolved.imperialScript();
        m.stockState = MapObjectState.setStockFlag(m.stockState, "lootSummary", ContainerIdentityApi.safeToken(resolved.summary()));
        world.mapObjects.add(m);
        if (world.inBounds(target.x,target.y)) world.tiles[target.x][target.y] = 'r';

        int groundCount = createGroundLootContainerNear(target, corpseId, resolved.groundItemNames(), cause);
        DebugLog.audit("CORPSE_CONTAINER_CREATED", "target=" + target.name + " faction=" + target.faction + " container=" + cid + " corpseItems=" + corpseLoot.size() + " groundItems=" + groundCount + " script=" + resolved.imperialScript() + " cause=" + cause + " summary=" + resolved.summary() + " state=" + stateSummary());
        return "Corpse container " + cid + " holds " + corpseLoot.size() + " item(s), nearby ground drops " + groundCount + ", script " + resolved.imperialScript() + ".";
    }
```

```java
    void updateLoadingPhase(String status, String detail, int progress) {
        String safeStatus = status == null ? "Loading..." : status;
        String safeDetail = detail == null ? "" : detail;
        int safeProgress = Math.max(0, Math.min(99, progress));
        SwingUtilities.invokeLater(() -> {
            loadingStatus = safeStatus;
            loadingDetail = safeDetail;
            loadingProgress = Math.max(loadingProgress, safeProgress);
            lastLoadingPulseMillis = System.currentTimeMillis();
            repaint();
```

```java
    void applyNameLockedProfileUnlocks(JobProfile chosenJob) {
```

```java
    List<String> nameLockedProfileStartingItems(NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry e) {
        ArrayList<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
        if (e == null) return out;
        out.add(e.displayName + " profile sigil");
        out.add(e.title + " dossier token");
        for (String flag : e.unlockFlags) {
            String clean = flag == null ? "" : flag.replace("PROFILE_PORTRAIT_", "").replace('_', ' ').toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).trim();
            if (!clean.isEmpty() && out.size() < 4) out.add("Profile unlock: " + clean);
        }
        return out;
    }
```

Name: materializeEquippedClothingItem
SHA256: 72ea4e5c43aefc3b79945d9e5ffeaa72c0159d4543945d28087f125251aa169f

```java
    void materializeEquippedClothingItem(JobProfile chosenJob) {
        if (equippedClothing == null || equippedClothing.name == null || equippedClothing.name.isBlank()) return;
        String baseName = equippedClothing.name;
        String equippedName = baseName + (equippedClothing.damaged && !baseName.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("damaged") ? " (damaged)" : "");

        // Starting clothing lives on the paper doll, not as a duplicate carried stack.
        for (int i = inventory.size() - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
            String carried = inventory.get(i);
            if (ItemQuality.namesMatch(carried, baseName) || ItemQuality.namesMatch(carried, equippedName)) {
                inventory.remove(i);
                removeContainerInstanceByName(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, carried);
            }
        }

        String cid = equipmentContainerIdForSlot(2);
        ContainerRecord slot = ensureContainer(cid, "Player equipment slot: Clothing");
        boolean alreadyTracked = false;
        for (String id : new ArrayList<String>(slot.itemInstanceIds)) {
            ItemInstance inst = itemInstances.get(id);
            if (inst != null && (ItemQuality.namesMatch(inst.displayName, baseName) || ItemQuality.namesMatch(inst.displayName, equippedName))) {
                alreadyTracked = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if (!alreadyTracked) {
            ItemProvenanceRecord pr = ItemProvenanceRecord.startingKit(equippedName, chosenJob, world, turn);
            addItemToContainerResult(cid, "Player equipment slot: Clothing", equippedName, pr, null, "starting clothing equipped on character paper doll");
        }
        selectedEquipmentSlotIndex = 2;
        DebugLog.audit("STARTING_CLOTHING_EQUIPPED", "item=" + equippedName + " slot=Clothing inventoryContainsBase=" + inventory.contains(baseName) + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void applyJobProfile(JobProfile profile) {
        for (Map.Entry<String,Integer> e : profile.statBonuses.entrySet()) {
            active.stats.put(e.getKey(), active.stats.getOrDefault(e.getKey(), 0) + e.getValue());
        }
        for (Map.Entry<String,Integer> e : profile.statPenalties.entrySet()) {
            active.stats.put(e.getKey(), Math.max(1, active.stats.getOrDefault(e.getKey(), 0) + e.getValue()));
        }
        if (profile.faction != Faction.NONE) {
            factionStanding.put(profile.faction, factionStanding.getOrDefault(profile.faction, 0) + 5);
        }
        DebugLog.audit("JOB_APPLY", profile.name + " bonuses=" + profile.bonusText() + " clothing=" + profile.clothingName + " faction=" + profile.faction.label);
    }
```

```java
    ZoneType auditZoneType() {
```

```java
    void setAuditZoneTypeIndex(int idx) {
        ZoneType[] values = ZoneType.values();
        if (values.length == 0) return;
        auditZoneTypeIndex = Math.floorMod(idx, values.length);
        auditZoneDropdownOpen = false;
        int visible = Math.max(3, Math.min(5, values.length));
        if (auditZoneTypeIndex < auditZoneButtonScroll) auditZoneButtonScroll = auditZoneTypeIndex;
        if (auditZoneTypeIndex >= auditZoneButtonScroll + visible) auditZoneButtonScroll = auditZoneTypeIndex - visible + 1;
        auditZoneButtonScroll = Math.max(0, Math.min(Math.max(0, values.length - visible), auditZoneButtonScroll));
        regenerateSectorAuditWorld("select audit zone type");
    }
```

Name: regenerateSectorAuditWorld
SHA256: 1dd2e3955be6d839d216fe2c3e384ab48be2f08321e6562b85413adaab386f04

```java
    void regenerateSectorAuditWorld(String reason) {
        long previousSeed = auditSeed;
        if (reason != null && reason.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("reroll")) auditSeed = System.currentTimeMillis() ^ (auditSeed * 31L);
        WorldSetupSettings previousSettings = WorldGenerationApi.settings().copy();
        try {
            WorldSetupSettings auditSettings = auditSettings();
            WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(auditSettings);
            Dimension d = WorldGenerationApi.zoneSliceSize(auditSeed);
            World w = new World(auditSeed, d.width, d.height);
            w.zoneType = auditZoneType();
            w.sewerLayer = auditSewerLayer;
            w.hiveName = "Audit Arcology";
            w.sectorName = "Zone Audit";
            w.zoneName = "Zone Audit " + w.zoneType.label + (w.sewerLayer ? " Sewer" : " Floor");
            w.zoneHistory = "Full-bright Zone Audit slice generated outside character play for placement and obstruction inspection.";
            SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.begin();
            try { w.generate(); }
            finally { auditTraceSteps = SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.end(); }
            if (auditTraceSteps == null) auditTraceSteps = new ArrayList<>();
            if (auditTraceSteps.isEmpty()) auditTraceSteps.add(new SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.Step(0, "FINAL", "Final generated world captured without intermediate trace records.", Math.max(0, w.w/2), Math.max(0, w.h/2), false, SectorGenerationTraceAuthority.snapshot(w)));
            auditTracePlaying = true;
            auditTraceIndex = 0;
            auditTraceLastAdvance = System.currentTimeMillis();
            auditWorld = auditTraceSteps.get(0).world;
            auditFindingIndex = 0;
            refreshSectorAuditSnapshot(auditSettings, previousSeed, "trace start: " + reason);
            DebugLog.audit("ZONE_AUDIT", auditReport);
            logEvent("Zone audit trace generated: " + w.zoneType.label + " steps=" + auditTraceSteps.size() + " finalRooms=" + w.rooms.size() + ".");
        } finally {
            WorldGenerationApi.setActiveSettings(previousSettings);
        }
        repaint();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:47-77
Kind: method
Name: deleteSelectedWorldDefinition
SHA256: 69783cf2cd63831560c8ebf651509155344267a2ede4a0fcb34a42328e6e990c

```java
    void deleteSelectedWorldDefinition() {
        if (availableWorlds == null || availableWorlds.isEmpty()) {
            lastWorldSetupReport = "No saved world definition is selected for deletion.";
            repaint();
            return;
        }
        int idx = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedWorldIndex, availableWorlds.size() - 1));
        WorldSaveInfo info = availableWorlds.get(idx);
        String summary = info == null ? "unknown world" : info.summaryLine();
        try {
            Path worldDir = CampaignWorldApi.worldDir().toAbsolutePath().normalize();
            Path target = info.path.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
            String name = target.getFileName() == null ? "" : target.getFileName().toString();
            if (!target.startsWith(worldDir) || !name.endsWith(".mechworld")) {
                throw new IOException("Refusing to delete path outside generated-world directory: " + target);
            }
            Files.deleteIfExists(target);
            DebugLog.audit("WORLD_DEFINITION_DELETED", "path=" + target + " summary=" + summary);
            lastWorldSetupReport = "Deleted world definition: " + summary;
        } catch (Exception ex) {
            DebugLog.error("WORLD_DEFINITION_DELETE_FAILED", "Could not delete selected world definition: " + summary, ex);
            lastWorldSetupReport = "Could not delete selected world definition: " + ex.getMessage();
        }
        availableWorlds = WorldSaveInfo.listExistingWorlds();
        selectedWorldIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(idx, Math.max(0, availableWorlds.size() - 1)));
        if (availableWorlds.isEmpty()) {
            pendingWorldSetup = WorldSetupSettings.standard();
            lastWorldSetupReport += " No saved worlds remain; generate a new arcology world before character creation.";
        }
        repaint();
    }
```

SHA256: 27412b07224109d75a7d0256d8da26faee09e887cf14c916e643a415ae3f3b96

```java
    void drawSectorAuditSurface(Graphics2D g) {
        advanceAuditTracePlaybackIfNeeded();
        if (auditWorld == null) regenerateSectorAuditWorld("draw missing audit world");
        UiLayout L = uiLayout();
        Rectangle map = L.map;
        g.setFont(auditAsciiFont());
        int cellW = auditMapCellW(g);
        int cellH = auditMapCellH(g);
        int cols = Math.max(1, (map.width - 18) / Math.max(1, cellW));
        int rows = Math.max(1, (map.height - 18) / Math.max(1, cellH));
        int camX = auditWorld == null ? 0 : Math.max(0, Math.min(auditWorld.w - cols, auditCursorX - cols / 2));
        int camY = auditWorld == null ? 0 : Math.max(0, Math.min(auditWorld.h - rows, auditCursorY - rows / 2));
        g.setColor(Color.BLACK);
        g.fillRect(map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height);
        drawSlicedFrame(g, map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height, "inner");
        stampUiFrameId(g, "F", "zone-audit-map", map.x, map.y, map.width, map.height);
        Shape oldClip = g.getClip();
        g.setClip(map.x + 7, map.y + 7, map.width - 14, map.height - 14);
        int ox = map.x + 10;
        int oy = sectorAuditTileIconMode() ? map.y + 10 : map.y + 10 + g.getFontMetrics(auditAsciiFont()).getAscent();
        if (auditWorld != null) {
            World oldWorld = world;
            boolean[][] oldVisibleTiles = visibleTiles;
            boolean[][] oldRememberedTiles = rememberedTiles;
            world = auditWorld;
            visibleTiles = SectorAuditRuntimeAuthority.fullBrightMask(auditWorld);
            rememberedTiles = visibleTiles;
            try {
                for (int sy = 0; sy < rows; sy++) {
                    int y = camY + sy;
                    if (y < 0 || y >= auditWorld.h) continue;
                    for (int sx = 0; sx < cols; sx++) {
                        int x = camX + sx;
                        if (x < 0 || x >= auditWorld.w) continue;
                        char ch = auditWorld.tiles[x][y];
                        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) drawMapTileIcon(g, ch, x, y, ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH, cellW, cellH, 1.0f, true);
                        else { g.setColor(colorForTile(x, y, ch)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(ch), ox + sx * cellW, oy + sy * cellH); }
                    }
                }
                if (auditWorld.mapObjects != null) {
                    for (MapObjectState mo : auditWorld.mapObjects) {
                        if (mo == null || mo.x < camX || mo.y < camY || mo.x >= camX + cols || mo.y >= camY + rows) continue;
                        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) drawMapFeatureIcon(g, mo, ox + (mo.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (mo.y - camY) * cellH, cellW, cellH, new Color(100, 210, 160, 70));
                        else { g.setColor(new Color(170, 215, 155)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(mo.glyph), ox + (mo.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (mo.y - camY) * cellH); }
                    }
                }
                if (auditWorld.lightSources != null) drawZoneLightFixtureObjects(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                if (auditWorld.hazardWarnings != null) drawEnvironmentalHazardOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                if (auditWorld.trapRecords != null) drawTrapWarningOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                if (auditWorld.npcs != null) {
                    for (NpcEntity npc : auditWorld.npcs) {
                        if (npc == null || npc.x < camX || npc.y < camY || npc.x >= camX + cols || npc.y >= camY + rows) continue;
                        if (sectorAuditTileIconMode()) drawNpcMapIcon(g, npc, ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH, cellW, cellH);
                        else { g.setColor(npcColor(npc.faction)); g.drawString(String.valueOf(npc.symbol), ox + (npc.x - camX) * cellW, oy + (npc.y - camY) * cellH); }
                    }
                }
                drawSectorAuditDiagnosticOverlays(g, camX, camY, cols, rows, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                drawSectorAuditTraceMarker(g, camX, camY, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
                drawZoneAuditGenerationLogOverlay(g, map, camX, camY, ox, oy, cellW, cellH);
            } finally { world = oldWorld; visibleTiles = oldVisibleTiles; rememberedTiles = oldRememberedTiles; }
            int sx = auditCursorX - camX, sy = auditCursorY - camY;
            if (sx >= 0 && sy >= 0 && sx < cols && sy < rows) {
                int rx = ox + sx * cellW, ry = oy + sy * cellH;
                g.setColor(new Color(245, 210, 95));
                g.drawRect(rx - 2, ry - 2, cellW + 4, cellH + 4);
                g.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry - 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + Math.max(2, cellH/4));
                g.drawLine(rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH + 5, rx + cellW/2, ry + cellH - Math.max(2, cellH/4));
                g.drawLine(rx - 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
                g.drawLine(rx + cellW + 5, ry + cellH/2, rx + cellW - Math.max(2, cellW/4), ry + cellH/2);
            }
        }
        g.setClip(oldClip);
        drawSectorAuditCommandPanel(g, L);
        drawSectorAuditInfoPanel(g, L);
        drawSectorAuditZoneDropdown(g, L);
    }
```

Name: auditTileInspectionLines
SHA256: 2cfc062922bba34fcb996b9153178a262e4765835e0645070ecd722be54abccf

```java
    java.util.List<String> auditTileInspectionLines(int x, int y) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        if (auditWorld == null || !auditWorld.inBounds(x, y)) return lines;
        char ch = auditWorld.tiles[x][y];
        int roomId = auditWorld.roomIdAt(x, y);
        RoomProfile rp = roomId >= 0 && roomId < auditWorld.roomProfiles.size() ? auditWorld.roomProfiles.get(roomId) : null;
        Faction owner = auditWorld.roomFaction(roomId);
        CompiledTileDescriptor d = TileDataCompilationAuthority.resolve(auditWorld, x, y, ch);
        lines.add("Observed tile: glyph '" + ch + "' floor/wall layer=" + (d == null ? "unknown" : d.baseLayer + "/" + d.family) + " roomId=" + roomId + " owner=" + (owner == null ? "none" : owner.label) + ".");
        if (rp != null) lines.add("Room: " + rp.name + " — " + rp.descriptor + " features=" + rp.featureText + ".");
        ArrayList<String> occupants = new ArrayList<>();
        NpcEntity npc = auditWorld.npcAt(x, y);
        if (npc != null) occupants.add("entity=" + npc.name + " / " + npc.role + " / " + (npc.faction == null ? "none" : npc.faction.label));
        MapObjectState mo = auditWorld.mapObjectAt(x, y);
        if (mo != null) occupants.add("object=" + mo.summary() + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForMapObject(mo));
        if (auditWorld.lightSources != null) for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : auditWorld.lightSources) if (l != null && l.x == x && l.y == y) occupants.add("light=" + l.stockState() + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForLight(l));
        if (auditWorld.trapRecords != null) for (TrapRecord t : auditWorld.trapRecords) if (t != null && t.x == x && t.y == y) occupants.add("trap=" + t.label + " / " + t.type + " / " + t.state + " / effect=" + t.effect + " severity=" + t.severity + " | assetId=" + ObjectSemanticAssetAuthority.assetIdForTrap(t));
        if (auditWorld.hazardWarnings != null) for (EnvironmentalHazardRecord hz : auditWorld.hazardWarnings) if (hz != null && hz.x == x && hz.y == y) occupants.add("hazard=" + hz.label + " / " + hz.severityText() + " / " + hz.warningText());
        if (occupants.isEmpty()) lines.add("Tile contents: no entity, object/container, light, trap, or hazard record on the selected cell.");
        else lines.addAll(occupants);
        return lines;
    }
```

```java
    boolean auditTileHasInteractable(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null) return false;
        MapObjectState mo = auditWorld.mapObjectAt(x, y);
        if (mo != null) return true;
        char ch = auditWorld.inBounds(x, y) ? auditWorld.tiles[x][y] : 0;
        return auditWorld.isDoorSymbol(ch) || ch == 'S' || ch == 'E' || ch == 'v' || ch == '<' || ch == '>';
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard6.txt:901-910
Kind: method
Name: auditTileHasContainer
SHA256: 8fff70467a79cc688e50ba519dc4f45eb93d8e3fee5b952d2a4d88e9bd2d5061

```java
    boolean auditTileHasContainer(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null || auditWorld.mapObjects == null) return false;
        for (MapObjectState mo : auditWorld.mapObjects) {
            if (mo == null || mo.x != x || mo.y != y) continue;
            String low = ((mo.type == null ? "" : mo.type) + " " + (mo.label == null ? "" : mo.label) + " " + (mo.stockState == null ? "" : mo.stockState)).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if (low.contains("container") || low.contains("crate") || low.contains("stock") || low.contains("vault") || low.contains("cache") || low.contains("corpse")) return true;
        }
        char ch = auditWorld.inBounds(x, y) ? auditWorld.tiles[x][y] : 0;
        return ch == 'b' || ch == 's' || ch == 'q' || ch == '?' || ch == '$' || ch == 'r';
    }
```

```java
        for (ZoneLightSourceRecord l : auditWorld.lightSources) if (l != null && l.x == x && l.y == y) return true;
        return false;
    }
```

```java
    boolean auditTileHasTrap(int x, int y) {
        if (auditWorld == null) return false;
        if (auditWorld.trapRecords != null) for (TrapRecord t : auditWorld.trapRecords) if (t != null && t.x == x && t.y == y) return true;
        if (auditWorld.mapObjects != null) for (MapObjectState mo : auditWorld.mapObjects) {
            if (mo == null || mo.x != x || mo.y != y) continue;
            String low = ((mo.type == null ? "" : mo.type) + " " + (mo.label == null ? "" : mo.label)).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
            if (low.contains("trap") || low.contains("mine") || low.contains("explosive") || low.contains("alarm")) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
```

```java
    boolean auditTileHasTransition(int x, int y, char ch) {

        if (auditWorld.isDoorSymbol(ch) && (ch == 'D' || x <= 1 || y <= 1 || x >= auditWorld.w - 2 || y >= auditWorld.h - 2)) return true;
        return ch == 'S' || ch == 'E' || ch == 'v' || ch == '<' || ch == '>';
    }
```

```java
    java.util.List<String> infopediaEntries(int tab) {
        ArrayList<String> out = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(tab) {
            case 0:
                for (ZoneType z : ZoneType.values()) out.add(z.label);
                break;
            case 1:

                }
                break;
            case 2:
```

```java
    java.util.List<String> infopediaDetailLines(int tab, String entry) {
        if (isAssetInfopediaTab(tab)) {
            return SemanticAssetInfopediaAuthority.detailLines(AssetManager.registry(), entry, selectedInfopediaAssetType(), infopediaAssetFilter);
        }
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        lines.add(entry);
        lines.add("Reference ID: " + tab + ":" + Math.abs(entry.hashCode()));
        lines.add("");
        if (tab == 0) {
            ZoneType z = zoneByLabel(entry);
            lines.add("Zone profile");
            lines.add("Description: " + (z==null?"Unknown zone.":z.descriptor));
            if (z != null) {
                int[] minmax = z.roomSize(new Random(3));
                lines.add("Generation role: " + zoneGenerationRole(z));
                lines.add("Room pattern: 20-30 rooms per slice; larger centered zone footprint; biased room dimensions around " + minmax[0] + "x" + minmax[1] + "; specials selected from zone-specific pools.");
                lines.add("Likely NPCs: " + likelyNpcText(z));
                lines.add("Likely fixtures: " + new String(world==null?new char[]{'o','u','t'}:samplePropsForZone(z)) + " — " + zoneFixtureMeaning(z));
                lines.add("Player warning: " + zonePlayerWarning(z));
                lines.addAll(EconomicTopologyFramework.zonePurposeLines(z));
            }
        } else if (tab == 1) {
            lines.addAll(roomInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 2 || tab == 3) {
            if (entry.equals("Item Quality Ladder")) {
                lines.add("Quality and value reference");
                lines.add("Every cataloged item can be described through the same eight-tier quality ladder. This entry is about tier meaning, not one specific object.");
                lines.addAll(ItemQuality.detailLines());
                lines.add("Gameplay use: quality modifies value, charges/usefulness, reliability, and social/economic weight. It also feeds production ceilings and provenance labels.");
            } else if (entry.equals("Quality Authority Layer")) {
                lines.addAll(QualityAuthorityApi.detailLines());
            } else if (entry.equals("Knowledge Tree Authority")) {
                lines.addAll(KnowledgeTreeApi.detailLines());
            } else if (entry.equals("Machine Tier Authority")) {
                lines.addAll(MachineTierAuthority.detailLines());
            } else if (entry.equals("Vendor & Shop Stock Rules")) {
                lines.add("Vendor and shop stock reference");
                lines.add("Scope: explains how trade offers are assembled and priced, not what any one item does.");
                lines.add("Traders draw visible stock from cataloged items and may bias stock by faction, zone, room, and trader role.");
                lines.add("Offer labels may carry quality prefixes: Junk, Shoddy, Common, Serviceable, Fine, Masterwork, Noble, or Archeotech.");
                lines.add("Buy prices derive from catalog base price, item quality, trader markup, and haggle discount. Sell prices use catalog value, then apply trader pressure.");
                lines.add("Current operational rule: purchased offers are materialized on a trader shelf container, then transferred into player inventory with provenance preserved.");
            } else if (entry.equals("Faction Variant Production Rules")) {
                lines.add("Faction manufacturing identity reference");
                lines.add("Scope: explains why two goods with the same base item may differ by maker, doctrine, quality, social meaning, lawful status, and production inputs.");
                lines.add("Formula: base draft recipe + faction manufacturing identity + quality authority + knowledge category + machine tier = generated faction recipe variant.");
                lines.add("Generated faction variants remain draft/provenance-facing for now; they are not wholesale-injected into the player workbench list.");
                lines.add("Civilian goods favor availability; military goods favor rugged durability; noble goods favor comfort/status; Mechanist Collegia goods favor throughput/efficiency with higher power and maintenance demands; scavver goods favor repairability with serious defect risk.");
                lines.add("Recipe knowledge is quality-bound. Machines cannot exceed their own quality ceiling even when the actor knows a better pattern.");
                lines.addAll(FactionManufacturingProfile.summaryLines());
                lines.add("Example generated faction variants:");
                lines.addAll(FactionRecipeVariantApi.sampleLines(8));
            } else if (entry.equals("Production Quality Ceilings")) {
                lines.add("Production ceiling reference");
                lines.add("Scope: explains the cap that keeps production honest instead of letting every recipe produce top-tier goods.");
                lines.add("Output quality is capped by the lowest relevant authority: recipe knowledge tier, machine tier, input material tier, facility tier, and worker/recruit competence.");
                lines.add("Example: a Junk Micro Assembler can only make Junk outputs even if the player owns better knowledge. The pamphlet may be holy; the machine remains a coughing brick.");
                lines.add("Example generated recipe previews:");
                lines.addAll(ProductionRecipe.sampleLines());
                lines.add("Current status: faction variants use these quality, knowledge, and machine authorities; input-material, facility, and worker ceilings remain explicit hooks that stay permissive until those ledgers carry quality tiers.");
            } else {
                ItemDef def = ItemCatalog.get(entry);
                if (def == null) {
                    lines.add(tab==2?"Item catalog gap":"Weapon catalog gap");
                    lines.add("This entry exists in the menu but is not cataloged. It needs a proper entry before expansion continues.");
                } else {
                    lines.addAll(def.detailLines());
                }
            }
        } else if (tab == 4) {
            lines.addAll(survivalInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 5) {
            lines.addAll(combatInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 6) {
            lines.addAll(bodyInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 7) {
            lines.addAll(medicalInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 8) {
            lines.addAll(heatInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 9) {
            lines.addAll(xpInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 10) {
            if ("Profile Special Unlocks".equals(entry)) {
                lines.add("Name-locked profile unlocks");
                lines.add("These entries are separate from random character generation. They require both the active operator profile and the finalized character name to resolve to the same registered profile.");
                lines.add("Unlocks grant profile dossier items, a knowledge entry, and a portrait source that is kept out of the ordinary portrait pool.");
                lines.add("Rare world seeding: inactive registered profiles may appear as visiting nobles in noble districts. The active profile key is excluded so the player does not meet a duplicate of themselves.");
                lines.add("");
                lines.add("Registered profiles: " + NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.entries().size());
                for (NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry e : NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.entries()) lines.add("- " + e.displayName + " // " + e.title + " // " + (hasKnowledge("Profile Dossier: " + e.displayName) ? "known" : "locked"));
            } else if (entry != null && entry.startsWith("Profile Dossier:")) {
                String name = entry.substring("Profile Dossier:".length()).trim();
                NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.Entry e = NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.match(name).orElse(null);
                lines.addAll(NameLockedProfilePortraitAuthority.infopediaLines(e, e != null && hasKnowledge("Profile Dossier: " + e.displayName)));
            } else {
            KnowledgeDef def = KnowledgeDef.get(entry);
            if (def != null) {
                lines.addAll(def.detailLines());
                lines.add("Status: " + (hasKnowledge(def.name) ? "KNOWN" : "LOCKED") + ". Spendable knowledge credits: " + knowledgeCredits + ".");
                lines.add("Unlock UI: open the Character Dossier Knowledge Tree. The Infopedia is now reference/audit only for doctrine entries.");
            } else {
                lines.addAll(knowledgeReferenceLines(entry));
            }
            }
        } else if (tab == 11) {
            CraftingRecipe cr = CraftingRecipe.byName(entry);
            if (cr != null) {
                lines.addAll(cr.detailLines());
                lines.add("Current status: " + cr.shortStatus(this));
            } else {
                lines.addAll(craftingReferenceLines(entry));
            }
        } else if (tab == 12) {
            lines.addAll(productionInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 13) {
            lines.addAll(auditInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 14) {
            if ("Defense Build Surface".equals(entry)) lines.addAll(DefenseBuildSelectionAuthority.buildSurfaceLines());
            else if ("Defense Semantic Audit".equals(entry)) lines.addAll(DefenseSemanticIntegration.infopediaLines());
            else if ("Passive Defense Effects".equals(entry)) lines.addAll(PassiveDefenseEffectsAuthority.infopediaLines());
            else lines.addAll(DefenseSemanticIntegration.detailLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 15) {
            lines.addAll(npcInfopediaLines(entry));
        } else if (tab == 16) {
            Faction f = factionByLabel(entry);
            lines.addAll(factionInfopediaLines(f, entry));
        } else if (tab == 17) {
            if (TileInfopediaAuthority.isHeader(entry)) {
                lines.add("Tile category");
                lines.add(entry.replace("--", "").trim());
                lines.add("Select a tile entry below this header to audit its glyph, descriptor, icon source, and allowed variants.");
            } else {
                lines.addAll(TileInfopediaAuthority.detailLines(entry, images == null ? null : images.tileArt));
            }
        } else {
            Faction f = factionByLabel(entry);
            lines.addAll(factionInfopediaLines(f, entry));
        }
        return lines;
    }
```

```java
    java.util.List<String> survivalInfopediaLines(String entry) {
        ArrayList<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
        switch(entry) {
            case "Calendar and Time":
                lines.add("Calendar and action-time reference");
                lines.add("Rule: 100 action turns equal one local hour; 26 hours make one day; 28 days make one month.");
                lines.add("Current time: " + timeText() + ". The absolute turn counter remains the save/log authority while the visible clock translates it into survival time.");
                break;
            case "Food and Water":
                lines.add("Food and water pressure reference");
                lines.add("Current reserves: food " + food + "/15, water " + water + "/15.");
                lines.add("One reserve is consumed every eight awake hours. Starvation/dehydration damage checks happen hourly only after a reserve reaches zero.");
                lines.add("Food and water items restore reserves through inventory use and are now intended to preserve item provenance until consumption.");
                break;
            case "Sleep and Exhaustion":
                lines.add("Sleep debt reference");
                lines.add("Current sleep debt: " + (sleepNeed / TURNS_PER_HOUR) + " hour(s) of 26 before collapse risk.");
                lines.add("Sleep debt grows by one hour per awake hour. Reaching 26 hours can cause exhaustion collapse and carried item loss.");
                lines.add("Cots allow 1-8 hour sleep chunks; sleeping costs food/water by the sleep-cost rule and may reduce fatigue or wounds.");
                break;
            case "Stimulants and Recovery":
                lines.add("Stimulant and short recovery reference");
                lines.add("Coffee and stim items reduce immediate sleep debt or fatigue pressure, but repeated abuse creates stimulant strain and later backlash.");
                lines.add("Current fatigue: " + fatigue + "; stimulant strain: " + stimulantStrain + ".");
                lines.add("Design rule: stimulants buy time; they do not replace food, water, sleep, or actual medical work.");
                break;
            case "Look and Examine":
                lines.add("Look and Examine reference");
                lines.add("Look gives immediate visible context for the selected tile: tile identity, ownership, light/noise, stacked contents, obvious NPC or object detail, and whether deeper examination is useful.");
                lines.add("Examine spends time to read the selected visible target more carefully. Repeating Examine on the same target within a few turns can reveal deeper threat, senses, condition, evidence, and interaction context.");
                lines.add("Boundary: Examine reports known or observable reads. It should not reveal hidden identities, private contract state, or internal records unless the world has exposed them.");
                break;
            case "Movement Planning":
                lines.add("Movement planning reference");
                lines.add("PLAN MOVE lets the player choose a movement endpoint, preview the route, see hazards, and confirm instead of relying only on directional movement.");
                lines.add("Movement mode changes range, time cost, noise, fatigue, and observation. The preview divides long routes into action chunks based on the current movement mode.");
                lines.add("Current movement: " + movementModeLabel() + ", range " + movementModeRange() + ", cost " + movementTurnCost() + " turn(s) per tile.");
                break;
            case "Interaction Approach Planning":
                lines.add("Interaction approach planning reference");
                lines.add("When a selected interaction target is too far away, the interaction preflight can nominate a reachable adjacent approach tile.");
                lines.add("Starting PLAN MOVE from that context prefers the approach tile and labels the preview as an approach path, helping with doors, NPCs, pets, containers, machines, vendors, and other exact-range targets.");
                lines.add("If no approach tile is shown, the target may already be adjacent, blocked, unreachable, or not an interaction target.");
                break;
            case "Inventory and Transfer":
                lines.add("Inventory and transfer reference");
                lines.add("Item movement uses a shared preflight grammar: source, target, quantity, capacity, permission/access, quest/evidence protection, risk, and whether the move is reversible.");
                lines.add("Carried load currently reads " + carryStatusText() + ". Overflow blocks purchase and recovery actions before the item moves.");
                lines.add("Quest and evidence items are protected from ordinary sale so proof, delivery goods, journals, and active turn-in objects do not vanish through routine commerce.");
                break;
            case "Base Storage":
                lines.add("Base storage reference");
                lines.add("Claimed-base storage lets the player STASH the newest carried item and TAKE the newest stored item while standing inside the claimed room.");
                lines.add("Storage reports access, capacity, quest protection, and risk categories such as weapons, suspicious tools, commerce goods, survival reserves, and medical reserves.");
                lines.add("Current storage: " + baseStorage.size() + "/" + baseStorageCapacity() + " item(s). " + baseStorageRiskSummaryLine());
                break;
            case "Pet Care":
                lines.add("Pet care reference");
                lines.add("Companion animals expose ownership, adoption/sale context, hunger, thirst, rest, shelter, temperament, accessibility, and petting permission through Look and Examine.");
                lines.add("Petting requires a companion animal, safe temperament, visibility, and adjacency. Non-pet animals explain why contact is blocked instead of pretending to be inert scenery.");
                lines.add("Pet systems should feel like visible living systems, not hidden timers.");
                break;
            case "Context Prompts":
                lines.add("Context prompt reference");
                lines.add("Major panels show prompt lines using the current input binding label and the current context: ready actions are named, and blocked actions explain what is missing.");
                lines.add("Examples include moving adjacent before confirming Interact, selecting an item before inventory actions, choosing a build tile before construction confirmation, and needing an active trader before trade confirmation.");
                lines.add("Keyboard and controller prompts share abstract action names so rebinding and profile work can update prompts without rewriting every panel.");
                break;
            default:
                lines.add("Survival failure-state reference");
                lines.add("Failure comes from accumulated pressure: no food, no water, exhaustion, untreated wounds, bleeding, infection, or reckless stimulant use.");
                lines.add("Current pressure summary: wounds " + wounds + ", fatigue " + fatigue + ", bleeding " + bleeding + ", infection risk " + infectionRisk + ", pain " + pain + ".");
                lines.add("Design intent: survival should pressure long routes and bad decisions, not interrupt every few steps with petty meter chores.");
                break;
        }
        return lines;
    }
```

```java
    String factionTradeBiasText(Faction f) {
        if (f==null) return "unknown";
        String n=f.name();
        if (n.contains("MECHANIST COLLEGIA")) return "machine parts, sacred wire, data spikes, tool rolls, relays, and fabrication doctrine";
        if (n.contains("GANGER") || f==Faction.BANDIT) return "weapons, lock tools, stimulants, stolen goods, and cheap armor";
        if (n.contains("HIVER") || f==Faction.HIVER) return "rations, water, cots, basic tools, permits, and ordinary supplies";
        if (n.contains("NOBLE") || f==Faction.NOBLE) return "permits, fine rations, clean water, luxury scraps, legal shields, and high value services";
        if (f==Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS) return "paperwork, restraints, armor, rations, water, and restricted services";
        if (f==Faction.IMPERIAL_GUARD) return "military ration packs, field water, rugged tools, armor, and weapons";
        if (f==Faction.CIVIC_LEDGER_OFFICE) return "forms, permits, records, stamps, and legal access";
        if (f==Faction.SCAVENGER) return "junk tools, improvised water, dirty food, salvage, and cheap components";
        return "locally biased catalog stock and faction-site production profile";
    }
```

```java
    void flowSaveLoadButtons() {
        SaveLoadUiRects sl = saveLoadUiRects();
        if (sl == null) return;
        int rowGap = Math.max(4, scaled(4));
        int topButtonH = Math.max(18, Math.min(24, sl.manual.height / 10));
        int topButtonW = Math.max(104, Math.min(184, sl.manual.width / 4));
        int topY = sl.manual.y + 44;
        int rowStart = sl.manual.y + 84;
        int manualAvailable = Math.max(72, sl.manual.y + sl.manual.height - 18 - rowStart);
        int rowH = Math.max(18, Math.min(26, (manualAvailable - rowGap * Math.max(0, SAVE_SLOT_COUNT - 1)) / Math.max(1, SAVE_SLOT_COUNT)));
        int loadW = Math.max(92, Math.min(160, sl.manual.width / 5));
        int saveW = Math.max(76, Math.min(130, sl.manual.width / 6));
        int saveX = sl.manual.x + sl.manual.width - 14 - saveW;
        int loadX = Math.max(sl.manual.x + 14, saveX - 8 - loadW);
        int autoAvailable = Math.max(90, sl.auto.y + sl.auto.height - 18 - rowStart);
        int autoRowH = Math.max(18, Math.min(26, (autoAvailable - rowGap * 4) / 5));
        int autoButtonW = Math.max(112, Math.min(190, sl.auto.width / 3));
        int autoButtonX = sl.auto.x + sl.auto.width - 14 - autoButtonW;
        for (ButtonBox b : buttons) {
            if (b == null || b.label == null) continue;
            String l = b.label;
            if (l.equals("SAVE DIAGNOSTIC")) b.r = new Rectangle(sl.manual.x + sl.manual.width - 14 - topButtonW, topY, topButtonW, topButtonH);
            else if (l.equals("LOAD MENU")) b.r = new Rectangle(sl.auto.x + sl.auto.width - 14 - topButtonW, topY, topButtonW, topButtonH);
            else if (l.startsWith("MANUAL ") && l.endsWith(" LOAD")) {
                int n = Character.isDigit(l.charAt(7)) ? Character.digit(l.charAt(7), 10) : 1;
                b.r = new Rectangle(loadX, rowStart + (Math.max(1,n)-1)*(rowH+rowGap), loadW, rowH);
            } else if (l.startsWith("SAVE ")) {
                int n = Character.isDigit(l.charAt(5)) ? Character.digit(l.charAt(5), 10) : 1;
                b.r = new Rectangle(saveX, rowStart + (Math.max(1,n)-1)*(rowH+rowGap), saveW, rowH);
            } else if (l.startsWith("AUTO ")) {
                int n = Character.isDigit(l.charAt(5)) ? Character.digit(l.charAt(5), 10) : 1;
                b.r = new Rectangle(autoButtonX, rowStart + (Math.max(1,n)-1)*(autoRowH+rowGap), autoButtonW, autoRowH);
            }
            fitButtonInto(b, saveLoadButtonSafeRect());
        }
    }
```

```java
    void moveSelectedButton(int delta) {
        if (buttons.isEmpty()) return;
        selectedButton = Math.floorMod(selectedButton + delta, buttons.size());
        sounds.play("tab", options);
        DebugLog.audit("UI_BUTTON_SELECT", "selected=" + selectedButton + " label=" + buttons.get(selectedButton).label + " via keyboard | " + stateSummary());
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    boolean sectorAuditTileIconMode() {
        // The Zone Audit surface is a visual-generation inspection tool. If packaged tile
        // art exists, it should display that art even when the normal play map is set
        // to ASCII/gradient fallback, otherwise road/floor art regressions are hidden.
        return images != null && images.hasTileArt();
    }
```

```java
    void startCombatAnimation(String weapon, int x0, int y0, int x1, int y1, boolean hit) {
        if (world == null) return;
        combatAnimations.add(new CombatAnimation(weapon == null ? "bare hands" : weapon, x0, y0, x1, y1, hit, System.currentTimeMillis()));
```

```java
    boolean recentFeedExternalAwarenessEligible(String line) {
        if (line == null || line.isBlank()) return false;
        String low = line.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (low.startsWith("you ") || low.startsWith("your ") || low.startsWith("equipped ") || low.startsWith("equipment:") || low.startsWith("selected ")) return false;
        if (low.startsWith("inventory") || low.startsWith("cannot ") || low.startsWith("no direct use") || low.startsWith("finalized character:")) return false;
        if (low.contains(" player ") && (low.contains("moves") || low.contains("wait") || low.contains("equips") || low.contains("uses"))) return false;
        if (low.startsWith("world selected:") || low.startsWith("world generated:") || low.startsWith("profile-linked dossier")) return false;
        return true;
    }
```

```java
    boolean equipInventoryItemToPaperDoll(String item) {
        if (item == null || item.isBlank()) return false;
        int slot = inferredEquipmentSlotForItem(item);
        if (slot < 0) return false;
        if (slot == 2) { equipInventoryClothing(item); return true; }
        int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
        if (idx < 0) return false;
        String old = equippedItemForSlot(slot);
        if (old != null && !old.isBlank()) {
            ItemActionResult returned = transferFirstEquipmentItemBackToInventory(slot, old, "replaced equipped item from " + equipmentSlotNames()[slot]);
            if (!returned.success) addInventoryItem(old, ItemProvenanceRecord.found(old, world, turn, "previously equipped paper-doll slot"));
        }
        ItemActionResult moved = transferContainerItemResultAt(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, inventory, idx, equipmentContainerIdForSlot(slot), "Player equipment slot: " + equipmentSlotNames()[slot], null, "equipped by player into " + equipmentSlotNames()[slot]);
        if (!moved.success) { logEvent("EQUIPMENT: could not equip " + item + ": " + moved.playerText); return false; }
        setEquippedItemForSlot(slot, item);
        selectedEquipmentSlotIndex = slot;
        logEvent("EQUIPMENT: equipped " + item + " to " + equipmentSlotNames()[slot] + (old == null || old.isBlank() ? "." : "; previous item returned to inventory.") + " Defense bonus now +" + playerEquippedArmorBonus() + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("EQUIPMENT_TRANSFER", moved.auditText + " old=" + old + " armorBonus=" + playerEquippedArmorBonus() + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("equips " + item); repaint();
        return true;
    }
```

```java
    void applyScrollValue(String tag, int value, boolean log){
        value=Math.max(0,value);
        switch(tag){
            case "job-dossier": case "job-list": jobDossierScroll=value; break;
            case "inventory": inventoryScroll=value; break;
            case "inventory-info": inventoryItemDescriptionScroll=value; break;
            case "look-stack": lookStackScroll=value; break;
            case "character": characterScroll=value; break;
            case "factions": factionScroll=value; break;
            case "bases": baseManagementScroll=value; break;
            case "map-info": mapInfoScroll=value; break;
            case "infopedia-list": infopediaScroll=value; break;
            case "infopedia-detail": infopediaDetailScroll=value; break;
            default: return;
        }
        activeScrollTag=tag;
        if(log) DebugLog.audit("UI_SCROLL", tag+"="+value+" | mouse/key scrollbar input");
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:427-451
Kind: method
Name: transferContainerItemResultByInstanceId
SHA256: 410016570edf4d545496971158ae48fd8e4e284cfbe7238c8814baa43f036536

```java
    ItemActionResult transferContainerItemResultByInstanceId(String instanceId, String toContainerId, String toLabel, ArrayList<String> toLegacy, String route) {
        if (instanceId == null || instanceId.isBlank()) return ItemActionResult.fail("No item instance ID was supplied.", "container transfer by instance failed: blank id to=" + toContainerId);
        ItemInstance inst = itemInstances.get(instanceId);
        if (inst == null) return ItemActionResult.fail("That item record is no longer available.", "container transfer by instance failed: missing id=" + instanceId + " to=" + toContainerId);
        String fromContainerId = inst.containerId;
        String accessProblem = ActorAccessAuthority.containerTransferProblem(this, fromContainerId, toContainerId, route);
        if (accessProblem != null) {
            DebugLog.audit("ACTOR_ACCESS_BLOCK", "container transfer blocked from=" + fromContainerId + " to=" + toContainerId + " route=" + route + " reason=" + accessProblem + " state=" + stateSummary());
            return ItemActionResult.fail("Access denied: " + accessProblem, "actor access blocked from=" + fromContainerId + " to=" + toContainerId + " route=" + route);
        }
        ContainerRecord from = itemContainers.get(fromContainerId);
        if (from != null) from.itemInstanceIds.remove(instanceId);
        ItemProvenanceRecord prior = inst.provenance == null ? takeProvenanceForItem(inst.displayName) : inst.provenance;
        ItemProvenanceRecord moved = ItemProvenanceRecord.transferred(prior, inst.displayName, world, turn, route == null ? "moved between containers" : route);
        ContainerRecord dest = ensureContainer(toContainerId, toLabel);
        inst.containerId = dest.id;
        inst.provenance = moved;
        inst.provenanceUnitId = moved == null ? inst.provenanceUnitId : moved.unitId;
        itemInstances.put(inst.id, inst);
        if (!dest.itemInstanceIds.contains(inst.id)) dest.itemInstanceIds.add(inst.id);
        if (toLegacy != null) toLegacy.add(inst.displayName);
        rememberItemProvenance(inst.displayName, moved);
        DebugLog.audit("CONTAINER_TRANSFER", "item=" + inst.displayName + " from=" + fromContainerId + " to=" + toContainerId + " route=" + route + " instance=" + inst.id + " state=" + stateSummary());
        return ItemActionResult.ok(inst.displayName, inst.id, toContainerId, moved, inst.displayName + " moved to " + toLabel + ".", "container transfer by instance item=" + inst.displayName + " instance=" + inst.id + " from=" + fromContainerId + " to=" + toContainerId + " route=" + route);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:453-484
Kind: method
Name: transferContainerItemAt
SHA256: 9b47006b01fd8322f54a3d6c78c853d873fddda8ab4d86d2c0f8c99d5c8b4ee1

```java
    ItemInstance transferContainerItemAt(String fromContainerId, ArrayList<String> fromLegacy, int idx,
                                         String toContainerId, String toLabel, ArrayList<String> toLegacy,
                                         String route) {
        if (idx < 0 || idx >= fromLegacy.size()) return null;
        String accessProblem = ActorAccessAuthority.containerTransferProblem(this, fromContainerId, toContainerId, route);
        if (accessProblem != null) {
            DebugLog.audit("ACTOR_ACCESS_BLOCK", "legacy container transfer blocked from=" + fromContainerId + " to=" + toContainerId + " route=" + route + " reason=" + accessProblem + " state=" + stateSummary());
            return null;
        }
        String item = fromLegacy.remove(idx);
        ItemInstance inst = removeContainerInstanceAt(fromContainerId, idx, item);
        ItemProvenanceRecord prior = inst != null && inst.provenance != null ? inst.provenance : takeProvenanceForItem(item);
        ItemProvenanceRecord moved = ItemProvenanceRecord.transferred(prior, item, world, turn, route == null ? "moved between containers" : route);
        ContainerRecord dest = ensureContainer(toContainerId, toLabel);
        if (inst == null) {
            String id = nextItemInstanceId();
            inst = new ItemInstance(id, item, dest.id, moved == null ? "" : moved.unitId, moved);
            itemInstances.put(id, inst);
            dest.itemInstanceIds.add(id);
        } else {
            inst.displayName = item;
            inst.containerId = dest.id;
            inst.provenance = moved;
            inst.provenanceUnitId = moved == null ? inst.provenanceUnitId : moved.unitId;
            itemInstances.put(inst.id, inst);
            dest.itemInstanceIds.add(inst.id);
        }
        if (toLegacy != null) toLegacy.add(item);
        rememberItemProvenance(item, moved);
        DebugLog.audit("CONTAINER_TRANSFER", "item=" + item + " from=" + fromContainerId + " to=" + toContainerId + " route=" + route + " instance=" + (inst==null?"none":inst.id) + " state=" + stateSummary());
        return inst;
    }
```

SHA256: 03b487e617bffe5adfd3f016baa388910f040987db73101526403fcc96cc7ed3

```java
    void equipInventoryClothing(String item) {
        int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
        if (idx < 0) { logEvent("Cannot equip " + item + ": no carried copy found."); return; }
        Clothing old = equippedClothing;
        String oldItem = old == null || old.name == null ? "" : old.name + (old.damaged && !old.name.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("damaged") ? " (damaged)" : "");
        if (oldItem != null && !oldItem.isBlank()) {
            ItemActionResult returned = transferFirstEquipmentItemBackToInventory(2, oldItem, "replaced equipped clothing");
            if (!returned.success && old != null && old.name != null && !old.name.isEmpty()) addInventoryItem(oldItem, ItemProvenanceRecord.of(old.name, old.alignedFaction, "previously equipped clothing", world, turn, "existing equipped garment", "returned to carried inventory after clothing change"));
        }
        boolean damaged = item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("damaged");
        Faction f = factionForClothingItem(item);
        int base = damaged ? 26 : 46;
        int defense = damaged ? 1 : 2;
        if (f == Faction.CIVIC_WARDENS || f == Faction.IMPERIAL_GUARD) { defense += damaged ? 1 : 2; base -= 4; }
        if (f == Faction.MECHANICUS_CLOISTER_RED) { defense += 1; base += 2; }
        ItemActionResult moved = transferContainerItemResultAt(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, inventory, idx, equipmentContainerIdForSlot(2), "Player equipment slot: Clothing", null, "equipped by player as clothing");
        if (!moved.success) { logEvent("Cannot equip " + item + ": " + moved.playerText); return; }
        equippedClothing = new Clothing(item, f, Math.max(8, Math.min(70, base)), defense, damaged);
        selectedEquipmentSlotIndex = 2;
        logEvent("Equipped " + item + ". Identity=" + equippedClothing.alignedFaction.label + ", cover=" + equippedClothing.disguiseBase + "%, defense=" + equippedClothing.defense + ". Previous clothing returned to inventory.");
        DebugLog.audit("INVENTORY_EQUIP_CLOTHING", moved.auditText + " faction=" + f + " old=" + (old!=null?old.name:"none") + " state=" + stateSummary());
        advanceTurn("changes clothing"); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void applyMedicalItemEffect(String item, String low, int oldWounds, int oldFatigue) {
        int oldBleed = bleeding, oldInfection = infectionRisk, oldPain = pain;
        if (low.contains("bandage") || low.contains("field dressing")) {
            bleeding = Math.max(0, bleeding - 4);
            wounds = Math.max(0, wounds - 1);
        } else if (low.contains("antiseptic")) {
            infectionRisk = Math.max(0, infectionRisk - 6);
        } else if (low.contains("splint")) {
            pain = Math.max(0, pain - 2);
            stabilizeWorstLimb(35.0);
        } else if (low.contains("medkit") || low.contains("medicae")) {
            bleeding = Math.max(0, bleeding - 6);
            infectionRisk = Math.max(0, infectionRisk - 4);
            wounds = Math.max(0, wounds - 2);
            fatigue = Math.max(0, fatigue - 2);
            pain = Math.max(0, pain - 4);
            healWorstBodyPart(55.0);
        } else if (low.contains("injector")) {
            wounds = Math.max(0, wounds - 1);
            fatigue = Math.max(0, fatigue - 2);
            pain = Math.max(0, pain - 3);
        }
        logEvent("MEDICAL USE: " + item + " applied. Wounds " + oldWounds + "->" + wounds + ", bleeding " + oldBleed + "->" + bleeding + ", infection risk " + oldInfection + "->" + infectionRisk + ", pain " + oldPain + "->" + pain + ".");
        DebugLog.audit("MEDICAL_ITEM", "item=" + item + " wounds=" + oldWounds + "->" + wounds + " bleeding=" + oldBleed + "->" + bleeding + " infection=" + oldInfection + "->" + infectionRisk + " pain=" + oldPain + "->" + pain + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void dropSelectedInventoryItem() {
        String item = selectedCarriedInventoryActionItem();
        if (item == null) { logEvent("Inventory empty. Nothing to drop."); return; }
        if (item.equals("Construction supplies") && supplies > 0) { supplies--; logEvent("Dropped one Construction supply onto the floor. It may or may not still be there later."); }
        else if (item.equals("Food reserve") && food > 0) { food--; addInventoryItem("Dropped food ration", ItemProvenanceRecord.found("Dropped food ration", world, turn, "converted from abstract food reserve")); logEvent("Converted one abstract food reserve into a carried dropped food ration item."); }
        else if (item.equals("Water reserve") && water > 0) { water--; addInventoryItem("Dropped water ration", ItemProvenanceRecord.found("Dropped water ration", world, turn, "converted from abstract water reserve")); logEvent("Converted one abstract water reserve into a carried dropped water ration item."); }
        else if (PortableLightProfile.isLightItem(item)) {
            dropPortableLightItem(item);
        }
        else {
            int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
            if (idx >= 0) {
                ItemActionResult dropped = transferContainerItemResultAt(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, inventory, idx, CONTAINER_VOID_DISCARDED, "discarded item ledger", null, "dropped by player in active sector");
                logEvent("ITEM DROPPED: Dropped one " + item + ". The item leaves your active carried stack. " + (dropped.provenance == null ? "Origin: untraced legacy item." : dropped.provenance.summary()));
                DebugLog.audit("INVENTORY_DROP", dropped.auditText + " state=" + stateSummary());
            } else logEvent("Drop failed: selected stack is not currently removable.");
        }
        selectedInventoryIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(selectedInventoryIndex, Math.max(0, stackedInventoryNames().size()-1)));
        advanceTurn("drops an inventory item."); repaint();
    }
```
