```java
    void usePortableLightItem(String item) {
        if (!PortableLightProfile.isLightItem(item)) { logEvent("That item is not a portable light source."); return; }
        int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
        if (idx < 0) { logEvent("Cannot light " + item + ": no carried copy found."); return; }
        PortableLightProfile p = PortableLightProfile.profile(item);
        if (p == null) { logEvent("Cannot light " + item + ": no light profile registered."); return; }
        if (p.consumedOnUse) {
            ItemActionResult consumed = transferContainerItemResultAt(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, inventory, idx, CONTAINER_VOID_CONSUMED, "portable light ignition ledger", null, "activated as disposable portable light");
            if (!consumed.success) { logEvent("Cannot activate " + item + ": " + consumed.playerText); return; }
        }
        activePortableLightItem = p.name;
        activePortableLightWorn = p.wearable;
        activePortableLightExpiresTurn = turn + Math.max(1, p.durationTurns);
        lastPortableLightReport = (p.wearable ? "WORN LIGHT: " : "CARRIED LIGHT: ") + p.name + " radius " + p.radius + " for about " + Math.max(1, p.durationTurns / TURNS_PER_HOUR) + " hour(s). " + p.note;
        logEvent(lastPortableLightReport);
        DebugLog.audit("PORTABLE_LIGHT_USE", "item=" + p.name + " radius=" + p.radius + " expires=" + activePortableLightExpiresTurn + " worn=" + p.wearable + " state=" + stateSummary());
        sensoryCacheWorld = null;
        advanceTurn("activates " + p.name + "."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void dropPortableLightItem(String item) {

        PortableLightProfile p = PortableLightProfile.profile(item);
```

SHA256: 5efaec396d58820d23017250eedbfd94f965a42342932e0ad85912a709339f2e

```java
    void throwSelectedPortableLight() {
        String item = selectedInventoryItemName();
        if (item == null) { logEvent("No selected item to throw."); return; }
        if (!PortableLightProfile.isLightItem(item)) { logEvent("THROW LIGHT blocked: selected stack is not a portable light source."); return; }
        int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
        if (idx < 0) { logEvent("THROW LIGHT blocked: selected light is not removable from inventory."); return; }
        PortableLightProfile p = PortableLightProfile.profile(item);
        if (p == null) { logEvent("THROW LIGHT blocked: no light profile registered for " + item + "."); return; }
        int fx = facingDx(), fy = facingDy();
        int range = Math.max(1, p.throwRange);
        int tx = playerX, ty = playerY;
        for (int step=0; step<range; step++) {
            int nx = tx + fx, ny = ty + fy;
            if (world == null || !world.inBounds(nx,ny) || !world.walkable(nx,ny) || world.npcAt(nx,ny) != null) break;
            tx = nx; ty = ny;
        }
        ItemActionResult thrown = transferContainerItemResultAt(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, inventory, idx, CONTAINER_VOID_DISCARDED, "portable light throw ledger", null, "thrown as active light source");
        int dur = p.remainingDuration(turn, activePortableLightItem, activePortableLightExpiresTurn);
        portableLights.add(new PortableLightInstance(p.name, tx, ty, p.radius, turn + Math.max(1, dur), portableLightWorldKey(), "thrown"));
        while (portableLights.size() > 48) portableLights.remove(0);
        if (p.name.equals(activePortableLightItem)) { activePortableLightItem=""; activePortableLightExpiresTurn=0; activePortableLightWorn=false; }
        lastPortableLightReport = "THROWN LIGHT: " + p.name + " lands at " + tx + "," + ty + ", radius " + p.radius + ", burn remaining about " + Math.max(1,dur/TURNS_PER_HOUR) + "h.";
        logEvent(lastPortableLightReport + " " + (thrown.provenance == null ? "" : thrown.provenance.summary()));
        sensoryCacheWorld = null;
        advanceTurn("throws a light source."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void consumeWakefulnessItem(String item) {
        int idx = inventory.indexOf(item);
        if (idx < 0) { logEvent("Cannot use " + item + ": no removable carried item found."); return; }
        ItemActionResult consumed = transferContainerItemResultAt(CONTAINER_PLAYER_INVENTORY, inventory, idx, CONTAINER_VOID_CONSUMED, "consumed item ledger", null, "consumed by player for wakefulness");
        if (!consumed.success) { logEvent("Cannot use " + item + ": " + consumed.playerText); return; }
        String low = item.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        int reduce = low.contains("narcotic") ? 12 : (low.contains("stim") ? 9 : 6);
        int strain = low.contains("narcotic") ? 3 : (low.contains("stim") ? 2 : 1);
        int oldSleep = sleepNeed, oldWounds = wounds, oldStrain = stimulantStrain;
        sleepNeed = Math.max(0, sleepNeed - reduce);
        stimulantStrain += strain;
        if (stimulantStrain >= 6) { wounds++; stimulantStrain -= 6; }
        DebugLog.audit("WAKEFULNESS_ITEM", "item=" + item + " sleepNeed " + oldSleep + "->" + sleepNeed + " strain " + oldStrain + "->" + stimulantStrain + " wounds " + oldWounds + "->" + wounds + " state=" + stateSummary());
        logEvent("Used " + item + ". Sleep need " + oldSleep + "->" + sleepNeed + "/" + MAX_SLEEP_NEED + ". Stimulant strain rises; cumulative abuse damages endurance.");
        advanceTurn("uses a wakefulness drug."); repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void runCargoNetworkAudit() {
        if (!baseClaimed) { logEvent("Cargo audit failed: no claimed base exists."); return; }
        int cap = cargoNetworkCapacity();
        if (cap <= 0) { logEvent("CARGO AUDIT: no cargo transfer system built. Build a Carrying Station, Supply Post, or Logistics Center to stage goods between bases."); return; }
        logEvent("CARGO AUDIT: tier=" + cargoNetworkTierName() + ", transfer capacity=" + cap + ", stored goods=" + baseStorage.size() + ", open businesses=" + openBusinessCount() + ". Reserved multi-base transfer will use this capacity as route bandwidth.");
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_CARGO_AUDIT", "tier=" + cargoNetworkTierName() + " cap=" + cap + " storage=" + baseStorage.size() + " bases=atlas state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void buyBusinessPermit() {
```

```java
    void openOrLicenseBusiness() {
        if (!baseClaimed) { logEvent("Business opening blocked: no claimed base exists."); return; }
        BaseObject obj = firstClosedBusiness();
        if (obj == null) { logEvent("Business opening blocked: no closed business-capable asset exists. Build a shop counter, medicae stall, storage crate, workbench, barrel, condenser, forge, or lab."); return; }
        if (consumeBusinessPermit()) {
            obj.businessOpen = true;
            obj.permittedBusiness = true;
            obj.businessHeat = Math.max(0, obj.businessHeat - 2);
            logEvent("BUSINESS LICENSED: " + obj.businessName() + " opens under a noble permit. Heat gain reduced; paperwork becomes its own small monster.");
        } else {
            obj.businessOpen = true;
            obj.permittedBusiness = false;
            obj.businessHeat += 4;
            gangHeat += 2;
            suspicion += 2;
            logEvent("ILLEGAL BUSINESS OPENED: " + obj.businessName() + " begins trading without a noble permit. Heat +2, suspicion +2. The ledger is a weapon pointed at you.");
        }
        recordPlayerNewsEvent(obj.permittedBusiness ? "licensed-service-opened" : "illegal-service-opened", obj.businessName(), Faction.NONE, (obj.permittedBusiness ? "licensed" : "unlicensed") + " service opened in claimed space", obj.permittedBusiness ? 2 : 6);
        DebugLog.audit("BUSINESS_OPEN", obj.businessName()+" permitted="+obj.permittedBusiness+" heat="+obj.businessHeat+" state="+stateSummary());
        repaint();
    }
```

```java
    void toggleRecruitGuardDuty() {
        if (!baseClaimed) { logEvent("Guard duty failed: claim a base before assigning security staff."); return; }
        if (factionRecruits.isEmpty()) { logEvent("Guard duty failed: no recruits available. Build cots and recruit workers first."); return; }
        RecruitWorker firstGuard = null, firstLabor = null;
        for (RecruitWorker r : factionRecruits) {
            if (r == null) continue;
            if ("security".equalsIgnoreCase(r.duty) && firstGuard == null) firstGuard = r;
            if (!"security".equalsIgnoreCase(r.duty) && firstLabor == null) firstLabor = r;
        }
        if (firstLabor != null) {
            firstLabor.duty = "security";
            logEvent("GUARD ASSIGNED: " + firstLabor.name + " moves to security duty. Defense rating now " + baseSecurityRating() + ".");
        } else if (firstGuard != null) {
            firstGuard.duty = "labor";
            logEvent("GUARD RELEASED: " + firstGuard.name + " returns to labor duty. Defense rating now " + baseSecurityRating() + ".");
        }
        DebugLog.audit("GUARD_DUTY_TOGGLE", "guards=" + securityStaffCount() + " labor=" + availableRecruitLabor() + " rating=" + baseSecurityRating() + " state=" + stateSummary());
        repaint();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:1591-1612
Kind: method
Name: applyBusinessPressureTick
SHA256: c19ce84e66a2fda717f571fb9cf9f9992276800ada9ae0be964d0ee289c67010

```java
    void applyBusinessPressureTick(boolean sleeping) {
        if (turn <= 0 || turn % TURNS_PER_HOUR != 0 || !baseClaimed) return;
        int legal = 0, illegal = 0, security = baseSecurityRating();
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) {
            if (!obj.isBusinessAsset() || !obj.businessOpen) continue;
            if (obj.permittedBusiness) legal++; else illegal++;
        }
        if (legal == 0 && illegal == 0) return;
        int heatGain = Math.max(0, illegal * 2 + legal - security / 4);
        if (heatGain > 0) {
            int oldH = gangHeat, oldS = suspicion;
            gangHeat += heatGain;
            suspicion += Math.max(0, illegal - security / 8);
            logEvent("BUSINESS HEAT: open commerce draws attention. Heat " + oldH + "->" + gangHeat + ", suspicion " + oldS + "->" + suspicion + ". Security rating " + security + ".");
        } else if (security > 0 && (gangHeat > 0 || suspicion > 0)) {
            int oldH = gangHeat, oldS = suspicion;
            gangHeat = Math.max(0, gangHeat - 1);
            if (security >= 6) suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion - 1);
            if (oldH != gangHeat || oldS != suspicion) logEvent("BASE SECURITY: patrols, locks, and alarms bleed off attention. Heat " + oldH + "->" + gangHeat + ", suspicion " + oldS + "->" + suspicion + ".");
        }
        maybeTriggerBaseRaid(security);
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:1614-1647
Kind: method
Name: maybeTriggerBaseRaid
SHA256: 3caa9b6464ab80364575e7357ecb79eba77bc2f8529756a5856ce8fe7266bf45

```java
    void maybeTriggerBaseRaid(int security) {
        int pressure = baseRaidPressure(security);
        if (pressure < 12) return;
        int chance = baseRaidChance(security);
        if (rng.nextInt(100) >= chance) return;
        String attacker = zoneRaidThreatName();
        int shield = 0;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if ((obj.symbol == 'H' || obj.symbol == 'T') && obj.armed && obj.charges > 0) { shield += obj.cover; obj.charges = Math.max(0, obj.charges - 1); }
        int damage = Math.max(1, 2 + rng.nextInt(4) - Math.max(0, security/5) - Math.max(0, shield/4));
        ArrayList<BaseObject> vulnerable = new ArrayList<>();
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if (obj.integrity > 0) vulnerable.add(obj);
        if (!vulnerable.isEmpty()) {
            BaseObject hit = vulnerable.get(rng.nextInt(vulnerable.size()));
            int old = hit.integrity;
            hit.integrity = Math.max(0, hit.integrity - damage);
            logEvent("BASE RAID: " + attacker + " hits " + hit.name + ". Integrity " + old + "->" + hit.integrity + ". Defense rating " + security + ", powered shield " + shield + ".");
        } else {
            logEvent("BASE RAID: " + attacker + " sweeps the claimed room, but no intact assets remain to smash. A grim efficiency.");
        }
        if (security >= 8) {
            gangHeat = Math.max(0, gangHeat - 3);
            suspicion = Math.max(0, suspicion - 2);
            logEvent("DEFENSE HOLDS: alarms, barricades, and crew response blunt the raid. Heat and suspicion drop as the attackers reassess.");
        } else {
            if (!baseStorage.isEmpty()) {
                String stolen = removeBaseStorageAtWithTrace(rng.nextInt(baseStorage.size()));
                logEvent("ITEM LOST: raiders seize " + stolen + " from base storage.");
            }
            fatigue = Math.min(25, fatigue + 2);
            wounds += 1;
            logEvent("DEFENSE FAILED: the raid leaves you battered. Wounds +1, fatigue +2. Build defenses or buy lawful cover.");
        }
        DebugLog.audit("BASE_RAID", "attacker="+attacker+" pressure="+pressure+" chance="+chance+" security="+security+" heat="+gangHeat+" suspicion="+suspicion+" state="+stateSummary());
    }
```

Name: addFactionMarketPressure
SHA256: d42073f44d8bfe274515db9171933a86717106efdeb2e2403ca49312fd364bf6

```java
    void addFactionMarketPressure(Faction faction, int amount, String reason) {
        if (faction == null || faction == Faction.NONE || amount <= 0) return;
        int security = baseSecurityRating();
        int mitigated = Math.max(0, amount - Math.max(0, security / 10));
        if (mitigated <= 0) return;
        int old = factionMarketPressure.getOrDefault(faction, 0);
        int next = Math.min(100, old + mitigated);
        factionMarketPressure.put(faction, next);
        if (next >= old + 3 || next >= 20 && old < 20 || next >= 40 && old < 40 || next >= 70 && old < 70) {
            logEvent("FACTION PRESSURE: " + faction.label + " resents your " + reason + ". Pressure " + old + "->" + next + ".");
        }
        DebugLog.audit("FACTION_MARKET_PRESSURE", "faction=" + faction + " amount=" + amount + " mitigated=" + mitigated + " reason=" + reason + " pressure=" + old + "->" + next + " power=" + playerFactionPower() + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void applyFactionMarketPressureTick(boolean sleeping) {
        if (turn <= 0 || turn % TURNS_PER_HOUR != 0 || !baseClaimed) return;
        int power = playerFactionPower();
        if (power <= 0) return;
        int open = openBusinessCount();
        int production = 0;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if (obj != null && obj.assignedRecipe != null && !obj.assignedRecipe.isBlank()) production++;
        int slowPressure = Math.max(0, (power / 25) + Math.max(0, open - 1) + Math.max(0, production - 1));
        if (slowPressure > 0) {
            Faction ambient = ambientRivalFaction();
            addFactionMarketPressure(ambient, Math.max(1, slowPressure - (sleeping ? 1 : 0)), "growing base power");
        }
        decayFactionMarketPressure();
        maybeTriggerFactionStrategicRaid();
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard7.txt:1889-1927

Name: maybeTriggerFactionStrategicRaid
SHA256: 17aba086ef1ee007ac2878392ed33b1f8fc3ce98d2395ef30da5a1ae5cd29339

```java
    void maybeTriggerFactionStrategicRaid() {
        Faction faction = highestFactionMarketPressureFaction();
        if (faction == Faction.NONE) return;
        int chance = strategicRaidChance();
        if (chance <= 0 || rng.nextInt(100) >= chance) return;
        int pressure = factionMarketPressure.getOrDefault(faction, 0);
        int security = baseSecurityRating();
        int power = playerFactionPower();
        String attacker = faction.label + " reprisal crew";
        int shield = 0;
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if ((obj.symbol == 'H' || obj.symbol == 'T') && obj.armed && obj.charges > 0) { shield += obj.cover; obj.charges = Math.max(0, obj.charges - 1); }
        int severity = Math.max(1, pressure / 18 + power / 18 - security / 10 - shield / 5);
        ArrayList<BaseObject> targets = new ArrayList<>();
        for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if (obj.integrity > 0 && (obj.isBusinessAsset() || obj.assignedRecipe != null && !obj.assignedRecipe.isBlank() || obj.symbol == 'k' || obj.symbol == 'q' || obj.symbol == 'G')) targets.add(obj);
        if (targets.isEmpty()) for (BaseObject obj : baseObjects) if (obj.integrity > 0) targets.add(obj);
        if (!targets.isEmpty()) {
            BaseObject hit = targets.get(rng.nextInt(targets.size()));
            int old = hit.integrity;
            hit.integrity = Math.max(0, hit.integrity - severity);
            logEvent("FACTION RAID: " + attacker + " attacks your market footprint and damages " + hit.name + " " + old + "->" + hit.integrity + ".");
        } else {
            logEvent("FACTION RAID: " + attacker + " searches the base, finds little to break, and leaves threats written in someone else's blood.");
        }
        if (!baseStorage.isEmpty() && severity > 1 && security < pressure / 6) {
            String stolen = removeBaseStorageAtWithTrace(rng.nextInt(baseStorage.size()));
            logEvent("ITEM LOST: " + faction.label + " raiders seize " + stolen + " to remind you who owns the market.");
        }
        int oldPressure = pressure;
        factionMarketPressure.put(faction, Math.max(0, pressure - Math.max(8, security / 2 + severity * 2)));
        if (security >= pressure / 6) {
            factionStanding.put(faction, factionStanding.getOrDefault(faction, 0) - 1);
            logEvent("DEFENSE HOLDS: your base survives the " + faction.label + " reprisal. Their pressure drops " + oldPressure + "->" + factionMarketPressure.getOrDefault(faction,0) + ", but relations sour.");
        } else {
            wounds += 1;
            fatigue = Math.min(25, fatigue + severity);
            logEvent("DEFENSE STAGGERS: the reprisal hurts. Wounds +1, fatigue +" + severity + ". More guards and powered defenses are advised.");
        }
        DebugLog.audit("FACTION_STRATEGIC_RAID", "faction=" + faction + " chance=" + chance + " pressure=" + oldPressure + "->" + factionMarketPressure.getOrDefault(faction,0) + " power=" + power + " security=" + security + " severity=" + severity + " state=" + stateSummary());
    }
```

```java
    void requestDoomModeToggle() {
        if (options == null) { logEvent("doom mode unchanged: options unavailable."); return; }
        if (options.doomModeEnabled) {
            applyQoL(GameplayQualityOfLifeAuthority.setDoomMode(options, false));
            return;
        }
        int choice = JOptionPane.showConfirmDialog(
                this,
                "doom mode is highly experimental and may cause instability.\n\nEnable the first-person 3D viewport wrapper for this profile?",
                "Enable experimental doom mode?",
                JOptionPane.YES_NO_OPTION,
                JOptionPane.WARNING_MESSAGE);
        if (choice == JOptionPane.YES_OPTION) {
            applyQoL(GameplayQualityOfLifeAuthority.setDoomMode(options, true));
            logEvent("doom mode assets/renderer unlocked. LWJGL dependency status: " + LwjglRenderBackendProbe.statusLine() + ".");
        } else {
            options.doomModeEnabled = false;
            options.save();
            applyQoL("doom mode remains OFF.");
        }
    }
```

```java
    void addGraphicsDropdownButtons(int x, int y, int bw, int gap) {
        if (graphicsDropdown < 0) return;
        Rectangle inner = graphicsDropdownInnerRect();
        if (inner.width <= 0 || inner.height <= 0) return;
        int rowH = Math.max(20, Math.min(30, scaled(27)));
        int yy = inner.y;
        if (graphicsDropdown == 0) {
            String[] modes = {"Windowed", "Borderless Windowed", "Exclusive Fullscreen"};
            for (int i=0;i<modes.length;i++) { final int idx=i; buttons.add(new ButtonBox(modes[i], inner.x, yy+i*rowH, inner.width, rowH-2, "Select " + modes[i] + " window mode.", () -> setWindowMode(idx))); }
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 1) {
            int available = DisplayResolutionAuthority.choiceCount();
            int visible = Math.max(1, Math.min(available, inner.height / Math.max(1, rowH)));
            int start = Math.max(0, Math.min(Math.max(0, available - visible), options.resolutionIndex - visible/2));
            for (int row=0; row<visible; row++) {
                final int idx=start+row;
                String prefix = idx==options.resolutionIndex ? "> " : "";
                buttons.add(new ButtonBox(prefix + DisplayResolutionAuthority.modeLabel(idx), inner.x, yy+row*rowH, inner.width, rowH-2, "Select detected/safe resolution " + DisplayResolutionAuthority.modeLabel(idx) + ".", () -> setResolutionIndex(idx)));
            }
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 2) {
            for (int i=0;i<GameOptions.PALETTE_NAMES.length;i++) { final int idx=i; buttons.add(new ButtonBox(GameOptions.PALETTE_NAMES[i], inner.x, yy+i*rowH, inner.width, rowH-2, "Apply palette globally: " + GameOptions.PALETTE_NAMES[i] + ".", () -> setColorPreset(idx))); }
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 3) {
            for (int i=0;i<GameOptions.DOWNSCALE_LABELS.length;i++) { final int idx=i; buttons.add(new ButtonBox(GameOptions.DOWNSCALE_LABELS[i], inner.x, yy+i*rowH, inner.width, rowH-2, "Use internal render scale " + GameOptions.DOWNSCALE_LABELS[i] + ".", () -> setDownscaleIndex(idx))); }
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 4) {
            for (int i=0;i<GameOptions.TARGET_FPS_LABELS.length;i++) { final int idx=i; buttons.add(new ButtonBox(GameOptions.TARGET_FPS_LABELS[i], inner.x, yy+i*rowH, inner.width, rowH-2, "Use target frame pacing " + GameOptions.TARGET_FPS_LABELS[i] + ".", () -> setTargetFpsIndex(idx))); }
        } else if (graphicsDropdown == 5) {
            for (int i=0;i<GameOptions.RENDER_QUALITY_LABELS.length;i++) { final int idx=i; buttons.add(new ButtonBox(GameOptions.RENDER_QUALITY_LABELS[i], inner.x, yy+i*rowH, inner.width, rowH-2, "Use render quality profile " + GameOptions.RENDER_QUALITY_LABELS[i] + ".", () -> setRenderQualityIndex(idx))); }
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard8.txt:347-370
Kind: method
Name: acceptJvmSettingsAndRestart
SHA256: 04500e4410d4547287e579decc99114cc8ab04f7eddd626a532eaad0b167c0e6

```java
    void acceptJvmSettingsAndRestart() {
        JvmRuntimeProfileAuthority.save(jvmRuntimeProfile);
        java.util.List<String> command = new ArrayList<>();
        String javaExe = Paths.get(System.getProperty("java.home", ""), "bin", isWindowsHost() ? "java.exe" : "java").toString();
        command.add(javaExe);
        command.addAll(jvmRuntimeProfile.buildJvmArgs());
        command.add("-cp");
        command.add(System.getProperty("java.class.path"));
        command.add(TheMechanist.class.getName());
        DebugLog.audit("JVM_RESTART", "Restarting with command=" + command);
        logEvent("Restarting with accepted JVM profile: " + jvmRuntimeProfile.targetLabel() + ".");
        try {
            new ProcessBuilder(command).inheritIO().start();
            shutdownRuntime();
            Window win = SwingUtilities.getWindowAncestor(this);
            if (win != null) win.dispose();
            System.exit(0);
        } catch (Throwable t) {
            DebugLog.error("JVM_RESTART", "Failed to restart with selected JVM profile.", t);
            jvmRuntimeNotice = "Restart failed: " + t.getMessage();
            logEvent(jvmRuntimeNotice);
            repaint();
        }
    }
```

Source: gamepanel-shard8.txt:1309-1331
Kind: method
Name: auditLoadingWatchdog
SHA256: 768215fd92fe4afb359bd2a1e13bed313baa0140a8fd48093ec2786c7f0341b4

```java
    void auditLoadingWatchdog() {
        long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
        long sinceStart = now - loadingStartMillis;
        long sincePulse = now - lastLoadingPulseMillis;
        if (loadingStep == 0 && sinceStart > 1200L && !loadingWatchdogReported) {
            loadingWatchdogReported = true;
            loadingWatchdogRepeats++;
            DebugLog.warn("LOADING_WATCHDOG_ZERO", "Loader remained at step zero for " + sinceStart + "ms. Forcing an audited progress tick. status=" + loadingStatus + " detail=" + loadingDetail);
            loadingStatus = "Watchdog forced loader heartbeat.";
            loadingDetail = "The loader had not advanced from step zero; an audited progress tick was forced so the UI cannot silently stall.";
            try { progressLoading(); } catch (Throwable t) { DebugLog.error("LOADING_WATCHDOG_FORCE_FAILED", "Forced loading heartbeat failed.", t); }
        } else if (loadingFinalizationRunning && now - loadingFinalizationStartMillis > 3000L && sincePulse > 2200L) {
            loadingWatchdogRepeats++;
            DebugLog.warn("LOADING_FINALIZER_WATCHDOG", "Background finalizer still running kind=" + loadingFinalizationKind + " elapsedMs=" + (now - loadingFinalizationStartMillis) + " step=" + loadingStep + " progress=" + loadingProgress + " repeat=" + loadingWatchdogRepeats);
            loadingStatus = "Still finalizing " + loadingFinalizationKind + "...";
            loadingDetail = "The background finalizer is alive. If this repeats for too long, diagnostic details will show the stuck phase rather than silently freezing.";
            lastLoadingPulseMillis = now;
        } else if (sincePulse > 2200L && sinceStart > 2200L && loadingProgress < 100) {
            loadingWatchdogRepeats++;
            DebugLog.warn("LOADING_WATCHDOG_STALL", "Loader pulse stale for " + sincePulse + "ms at step=" + loadingStep + " progress=" + loadingProgress + ". repeat=" + loadingWatchdogRepeats);
            lastLoadingPulseMillis = now;
        }
    }
```
